Increasing Numbers of Japanese and Puppet Troops in Malanyu 9

Over 700 Infantry and Cavalry Arrive from Jehol

Japanese Aircraft Conduct Daily Drills Along the Great Wall Line

Hundreds of Puppet Troops Stationed Near the Qing Tombs

Japanese Military Officials Machijiri and Shibayama Visit Gubeikou

(Tianjin) The Japanese airfield in Malanyu recently has six bomber and reconnaissance aircraft stationed there. They conduct daily drills along the Great Wall. Over 500 Japanese infantry soldiers and over 200 cavalry soldiers have arrived in Malanyu from the Jehol area. Heavy trucks have also been transporting artillery shells to the area for days. Residents are extremely frightened. Hundreds of puppet troops arrived near the Qing tombs early on the 4th to be stationed there. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Japanese side intends to use the return of Malanyu and Dolon as conditions for postal and vehicular traffic exchange with us, so they recently refused our reception. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) This morning, after paying respects at the Japanese cemetery in Beiping, Machijiri, Military Attache to the Emperor of Japan, accompanied by Japanese military official Shibayama, Chief of Staff Kikuchi of the Tianjin Garrison Army, and Matsui, head of the Chengde Special Affairs Agency, traveled by car to Gubeikou to inspect the local Japanese troops at about 10:00 AM. They are scheduled to return to Beiping on the 7th, and will go to Tianjin on the morning of the 8th. After a brief stay, they will proceed to the Yuyu area to inspect the Japanese troops. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Shibayama said that the recent arrival of Japanese troops in Malanyu is to protect the transportation of the Luan River's upstream, and the rumor that they are to protect Puyi's tomb sweeping is inaccurate. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) A dispatch from Miyun states that Lieutenant Colonel Kito, commander of a Japanese cavalry platoon, led a cavalry platoon from Yuyu to Malanguan on the evening of the 3rd. Upon arriving at the pass, he convened a meeting of village chiefs from nearby villages and raised four questions, asking them to answer, including: (1) How is the discipline of the local security team? (2) Do the police at the Public Security Sub-bureau have any illegal behavior? (3) Are there any bandits in the area? (4) Does the Chinese government have the ability to protect the local people? All four items must be answered accurately and signed, and it was said that if the villagers have any difficulties, they can jointly submit a written request, and the Japanese side will take responsibility for protection. The village chiefs understood the Japanese side's seductive tactics, and answered each item as follows: (1) There are no security teams stationed here. (2) Director Shi of the local Public Security Sub-bureau treats the villagers very peacefully, and illegal behavior is impossible to mention. (3) Banditry in the area has long been suppressed, and even if there are small bandits, the local defense has the ability to clear them. (4) The government does have considerable protection capabilities for the area. After the village chiefs answered, Kito took out a handgun and ordered them to sign as proof, and took it to Gubeikou on the morning of the 4th. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) In the Jiyu-Miyun area, at each small pass along the Great Wall, except for Zengjialu, where there are still a few puppet police who have not withdrawn, there are no traces of Japanese and puppet troops in the other small passes. In the near future, we will send police to station there to strictly prevent the import of drugs. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Shibayama is scheduled to go to Shanxi on the 8th. After finishing his tour in Taiyuan, he will go to Datong to visit the Yungang Grottoes. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) In the Gubeikou area, there are currently two companies of Japanese troops, five or six military police, over twenty Manchukuo police, and one customs clerk stationed. (6th Dispatch)

Feng Shoushan, Commander of the Yutian Security Special Agent Team, Has Softened 10

Removal of Defensive Works

Yin Rugeng Returns to Tongxian

(Tianjin) Feng Shoushan, the commander of the Yutian Security Team's Special Agent Team, planned to request an increase of several hundred men to his department. On the 4th, he guarded the city gate and piled up sandbags. The situation was serious for a time. Until noon on the 5th, Feng softened because he was aware that the provincial government had concentrated the Zunhua-Qianxi MinTuan on the Yutian border to block it. Feng Shoushan removed the defensive works on the afternoon of the 5th and listened to the authorities' downsizing. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Yu Xuezhong said that when Hu Xiewu was not dead, the Yutian Security Team had expanded to 2,300 men without permission. Now, as soon as they are downsized, 900 men will be discharged first, and the remaining 400 men will be commanded by Feng Shoushan, who will also have to be downsized in the future to completely resolve the issue without leaving any trouble behind. Even after the downsizing is completed and salaries are paid, they will be paid according to 1,000 men. Not a single additional one will be given. There is a rumor that there will be changes in the Yutian police team, but no report has been received yet, so it is probably inaccurate. When the team was organized, it borrowed five or six hundred Japanese guns. The Japanese side said they did not want them, and the provincial government did not covet this cheapness, so they returned them upon delivery. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Yin Rugeng returned to the Tongxian Public Office this morning to handle official business. According to reports, the Yutian Security Captain Han reported to Ping that the area was peaceful. The rumor that the Yutian Security Team had redeployed is inaccurate. The increase in Japanese troops in Gubeikou was a transit, and they left after a short rest. The issue of the withdrawal of puppet police from Nantianmen and other places has been handled by Huo Shi nearby, and I have telegraphed him because Shibayama went to Gubeikou. There should be no problems in general. Negotiations on the reception of Malanyu have not yet begun. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) A senior military officer said that the Yutian team police are holding onto transportation agencies, which is clearly resisting provincial orders and disobeying downsizing. In order to prevent police riots and disturbances, the Central Government has telegraphed the Ping Military Branch and Yu Xuezhong, Chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, to take effective precautions against police riots and local ruffians in the area to avoid their collapse and harm to the people. (6th Dispatch)

Song Zheyuan Telegraphed That Chahar East is Peaceful 11

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan telegraphed to Ping that his eye disease has healed and he plans to travel with Qin Dechun to Chahar East within a few days. Secretary-General Yang Zhennan will be appointed to act on behalf of the provincial government. The recent situation in Chahar East is peaceful. (6th Dispatch)

All Civilian Guns in the Three Northeastern Provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang Have Been Confiscated 12

A Total of 3.1 Million Guns

(Beiping) In order to prepare for war with Russia and prevent anti-Manchu and anti-Japanese forces, the Japanese Kwantung Army has been working hard to confiscate civilian guns in various parts of the Northeast. The confiscation has now been completed in the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang. Due to transportation relations, the confiscation has not yet been completed in Rehe. According to the rebel organization, the total number of guns confiscated is 1.5 million in Liaoning, 1.1 million in Jilin, and 500,000 in Heilongjiang, for a total of 3.1 million. The military power of 30 million people has been declared dead. (6th Dispatch)

Chiang Telegraphed Various Provinces to Suppress the Recruiting of Labor by Traitors 13

(Nanjing) Chiang telegraphed the local authorities of various provinces, saying that it has been reported that in Wangdu, Hejian, Tangxian, and Dingxian in Hebei Province, some people have recently been recruiting Chinese laborers under the pretext of gathering in Baoding for transportation to Tianjin and Dalian. He is deeply concerned that there will be traitors secretly colluding in the same way in other places. He hopes that they will be instructed to pay attention at all times and earnestly suppress it. (5th Dispatch)

Huang Fu Arrived in Nanchang Yesterday 14

(Nanchang) Huang Fu arrived in the province at 2:00 PM by train on the Nanchang-Xunyang Railway. Secretary-General Yang and Director Cai of the Executive Office, and Chairman Xiong all went to the station to welcome him. Huang stayed at No. 3 Gongyuan and immediately met with Chiang to report on the situation in North China. According to Huang, he came to report, and will then go to Beijing and return to his hometown. It is undecided whether he will go to Moganshan. When he went south, the situation in Chahar East, North China, was still good. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) According to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, Tang Youren accompanied Huang Fu to Jiangxi to meet with Chiang to report on North China diplomacy. There are no special missions. The date of return to Beijing is unknown. (6th Dispatch)

The Hebei Provincial Government Restrains the Tangshan Workers' Strike 15

Limit the Miners to Resume Work Within Three Days

Arrest Zhao Dazhong, the Leader of the Incident

Telegraph to Tao Shangming Not to Compromise with the Strikers

(Tianjin) This afternoon, the provincial government telegraphed Tao Shangming and Zhao Xun, instructing them not to compromise and agree to any conditions with the striking Kailuan miners. Zhao Dazhong and others, the leaders of the incident, should be arrested and sent to Tianjin for severe punishment by the provincial government. Yu Xuezhong said that last night, he instructed Zhao Xun and Zhao Lei by telephone to lead their respective departments to strictly protect the mine machinery, mine shafts, and foreign residences to prevent worker riots. On one hand, arrest Zhao Dazhong, and on the other hand, notify the workers to resume work within three days, otherwise they will be arrested. The Tangshan mine unrest is purely the work of a few troublemakers. This time, we will take a fundamental solution to avoid further labor unrest, even if there are sacrifices, we will not count it. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Hebei Provincial Government received a telegram from President Wang saying that the mine unrest should be resolved quickly so as not to expand the unrest. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Zhao Lei, the captain of the War Zone Security Team, and Zhao Dazhong have a colleague relationship. After the provincial government's telegram arrived in Tangshan on the 6th, Zhao signaled Dazhong to escape, so Zhao Dazhong has not appeared today. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Zhao Dazhong lost the faith of the striking miners of Tangshan Mine. When he goes out, he is accompanied by three Japanese and Korean people and a dozen gangsters, carrying weapons for protection. Zhao once lied to the Japanese side that he could pull in 50,000 workers from Eastern Hebei to be used by a certain party. Now that this matter has not been achieved, the Japanese garrison is also dissatisfied with him. On the 5th, the Japanese army entrusted Sugimura to express to the Tangshan gentry and merchants that Zhao Dazhong's actions were his personal affairs and had nothing to do with the Japanese side, so Zhao's power is isolated. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The striking workers of the Tangshan Mine borrowed money from the contractors on the 5th to maintain their livelihoods. Each person received two yuan in wages for this month. Because the workers lack daily necessities, they are more eager to resume work, just waiting for the mine to allow a change of conditions. The Kailuan Mining Bureau has armed its trusted workers to protect the mine shafts and machinery in the factory to prevent damage from the strikers. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Belgian Consul in Tianjin visited Yu Xuezhong and said that there are more than a hundred Belgian engineers and technicians in the Tangshan Kailuan mining area, and their lives and property must be protected. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) When the British Consul in Tianjin visited Yu Xuezhong on the 5th, he expressed that no matter how the officials handle the labor unrest, the most important thing is not to allow any conditions or issue any fees, which would lead to the bad habit of workers getting something for nothing. (6th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Kailuan strikers have not received wages for a long time, and their livelihood has become alarmed. Some violent workers, instigated by Zhao Dazhong, yesterday tied up dozens of contractor heads and extorted thousands of yuan to maintain their lives. The remaining conditions are still being worked on by all parties. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Correction: Yesterday's report from Tianjin stated that "[Japanese Consul-General in Tianjin Zhai Lansi visited Yu Xuezhong at the Hebei Provincial Government for the Kailuan coal mine labor unrest]." The word "Japanese" in the report was a mistake for "British". This is hereby corrected.

The Tianjin Huaxin Cotton Mill Strike Was Resolved on the Same Day 16

A Large Number of Workers Were Fired

(Tianjin) At about 6:00 AM on the 6th, some workers at the Tianjin Huaxin Cotton Mill planned to implement a strike in accordance with the methods of the workers at the Tangshan Huaxin Cotton Mill, demanding an increase in wages. The factory notified the Public Security Bureau to send a large armed police force to surround the factory and arrest several workers who advocated the strike. The factory, fearing a worker riot, immediately announced a layoff. After the authorities and the factory negotiated in the afternoon, Wu Jingui, Chen Wenzhang, and more than forty others were fired. The workers' night shift resumed work as usual. (6th Dispatch)

Men Bingyue Arrives in Ping to Discuss the Reorganization of Sun's Department 17

Tao Jun Stays in Suiyuan to Handle the Reception

(Beiping) Men Bingyue arrived in Ping this morning to talk about the reorganization of Sun's department. The issue has been largely completed and the aftermath has also come to an end. Yu Shiming's department will be transferred to the border between Henan and Shandong. The department opened to Linhe on the 30th of last month and arrived in Linhe on the 2nd of this month. The other departments are concentrated in the Sanshenggong area. Liu Yueting and Lu Fengnian's departments have been completely received and are determined to be transferred to the Hebei Province. The Liu department suffered the most losses in this battle. Ding Yuting's department has two brigades, Yang Ganqing's brigade is still in Ningxia, and Xia Weili's brigade has opened to Linhe. Yang Hou's small department is still rioting, and is being suppressed by the Shanxi-Suiyuan army. It is reported that they have returned to Baotou. In this compilation of Sun's army, a total of 12,300 guns were confiscated and 27,800 unarmed soldiers were received. Tao Jun is now in Suiyuan to handle reception matters. There are stations along the way from Suiyuan to Ningyuan. The areas around Wuyuan and Linhe have suffered extremely heavy losses. He has come to report everything to He and ask for instructions on how to reorganize Sun's army. Whether he will go west again will be decided after meeting with He. (6th Dispatch)

Wan Fulin Will Depart Soon for Inspection 18

(Beiping) Wan Fulin is scheduled to depart on the 10th of this month to inspect his subordinate troops. First, he will take the Ping-Sui Railway to Xuanhua to inspect Zhang Tingxu and Zhu Hongxun's divisions, and then go to the Guofang area of the Beining Railway to inspect Sun Dequan's department. After the matter is completed, he will transfer to the Ping-Han Railway to the Zhengding Yixian area to inspect Zhou Fucheng and Miao Chengliu's departments, which will take about two months. Wan has been inspecting his department at the Xiyuan inspection station for days. (6th Dispatch)

Chen and Li Send Staff to Siam to Welcome Xiao Focheng Back to Guangdong 19

The Southwest's Declaration on the Current Situation is Postponed

Zou and Hu Confer on the Draft Constitution and the Current Situation

Chen Jitang Expresses the Desire to Change the Guangdong Military System After Suppressing the Communist Bandits

(Hong Kong) Chen Jitang and Li Zongren decided to send a telegram to urge Xiao Focheng to return to Guangdong, and sent Xiao Songqin to Siam on the 8th to welcome Xiao. The Southwest's declaration on the current situation will be issued after Xiao returns to Guangdong and discusses it in detail. (6th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) Zou Lu arrived in Hong Kong by ship on the afternoon of the 6th and went directly to Hu Hanmin's residence to discuss the draft constitution and the current situation. (6th Dispatch)

(Hong Kong) The Guangdong Provincial Government has handed over the provincial system reform plan to the Guangdong Political Research Association for discussion. The association is scheduled to meet on the 11th. It is reported that the attitude towards the provincial system reform in the future will be based on the Southwest's opinions on the draft constitution. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Chiang Kai-shek has set up several methods for abolishing the two Southwest agencies and establishing military sub-committees, and telegraphed Chen in Guangdong. The content of the methods is to set up the Liangguang Military Sub-committee in Guangzhou, abolish the group numbers of the First and Fourth Army, uniformly change the names of the existing armies and divisions to avoid conflicts with the current numbers of the central government, appoint Chen Jitang as the director of the Military Sub-committee, Li Zongren as the deputy director, and select military commanders as members. The troops commanded by the Military Sub-committee will be based on the army or independent division as a unit. It is planned not to set up numbers such as the XXX Road, and it is also planned to set up an office of the Liangguang Military Sub-committee in Nanning. It is heard that Chen in Guangdong has expressed that the first step is to assist the central government in suppressing the communist bandits, and the second step is to change the Guangdong provincial military system to be consistent with the central government. As for the issue of the survival of the two agencies, it will be subject to the central government's orders, and Lin Yizhong is planned to be recommended to Jinjing to present his intentions. However, due to the different opinions of the Southwest veterans, further deliberation is still needed. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) It is rumored that Chen Jitang sent Yu Hanmou to attend the Nanchang Fifth Route Bandit Suppression Conference and put forward a total of 12 suggestions, the most important of which were the plan for the joint suppression, increasing military expenses for bandit suppression, and the air force's plan for bandit suppression. Chen also handed a personal letter on the Southwest current situation issue to Yu to present to Chiang. (6th Dispatch)

President Wang Explains the Dispatch of Inspectors 20

(Nanjing) President Wang discussed with the Central News Agency reporters on the morning of the 6th that the dispatch of special commissioners to inspect the various provinces is a common occurrence, such as the special dispatch of Foreign Minister and Minister of Justice Luo Wengan to inspect Xinjiang last year, and the special dispatch of Interior Minister Huang Shaoxiong, Deputy Chairman of the Mongolian Committee Zhao Pilian to inspect Inner Mongolia, which are previous examples. This time, the regulations were made to provide a basis for the special commissioners to work. The application has been submitted to the Central Political Conference by the Executive Yuan and approved for filing. The dispatch of special commissioners to inspect the various provinces will not conflict with the powers of the Supervisory Yuan. As for the selection of good or bad officials under the supervision, it is originally the responsibility of the superiors, and it is not only the Supervisory Yuan that can exercise this power. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Many members of the Legislative Yuan believe that the dispatch of special commissioners by the Executive Yuan has no legal basis and will also raise questions. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Wuhan Municipal Party Department telegraphed the central government, saying that the dispatch of special commissioners by the Executive Yuan has no legal basis, and requested that the Executive Yuan immediately revoke the original proposal. (5th Dispatch)

Zhu Jiqing Goes to Wuyuan and Linhe to Meet Fu and Wang 21

(Guihua Dispatch) Zhu Jiqing originally wanted to meet Fu Zuoyi in Baotou, but now he wants to inspect the situations in Wuyuan and Linhe. Zhu Jiqing went to Wuyuan and Linhe with Shi Huayan, the director of the Suiyuan Reclamation General Office, to meet with Fu Zuoyi and Wang Jingguo to discuss the relocation of the reclamation. (6th Dispatch)

(Beiping) After Zhu Jiqing and his party arrived in Baotou, they did not make the trip because in the Wuyuan and Linhe areas, Yang Hou's bandits had been robbing cars and kidnapping passengers for days. One day they went to Salazi County to visit the agricultural experiment farm and the Minsheng Canal, and planned to buy land in the county for reclamation. (6th Dispatch)

Huang Shaoxiong Goes to Jinci 22

Visits Sun Dianying

(Taiyuan) Huang Shaoxiong left by car for Jinci at 9:00 AM on the 6th to visit Sun Dianying. A total of four people went with him. They are scheduled to return to Taiyuan before 12:00 noon. Xu Yongchang is scheduled to host Huang for lunch at the Provincial Government. Huang plans to visit Yan Xishan on the 7th. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Beiping) Ningxia Dispatch: Ma Hongkui telegraphed to Taiyuan on the 6th to welcome Huang Shaoxiong to Ningxia for inspection. (6th Dispatch)

The Tibetan Office in Beijing Denies Welcoming the Panchen Lama Back to Tibet 23

(Nanjing) The person in charge of the Tibetan Office in Beijing said that according to a telegram from Lhasa, the three major monasteries in Tibet did not send representatives to Beijing to welcome the Panchen Lama back to Tibet. Anqin left Tibet for India last month with more than 50 followers. The outside world does not understand and believes that so many Tibetans leaving the country must be to welcome the Panchen Lama back to Tibet, but this is completely a misunderstanding. (5th Dispatch)

Legislative Yuan Meeting 24

Passes the Special Industry Incentive Law

(Nanjing) The Legislative Yuan held its 53rd meeting at 9:00 AM on the 6th, with 89 members including Shi Shangkuan in attendance. Sun Ke presided over the meeting and Liang Hancao served as secretary-general. The matters discussed were: (1) The Central Political Council's decision at its 399th meeting to separately amend the Organic Law of the Public Officials Disciplinary Committee, which was sent to the National Government and then transferred to the Legislative Yuan for handling. Resolution: Refer to the Legal System Committee for review. (2) Review the draft temporary organic regulations of the National Beiping Palace Museum. Resolution: Refer to the Legal System Committee for review. (3) Review the general budget of local revenue and expenditure for the 22nd year of Shandong Province. Resolution: Refer to the Finance Committee for review. (4) Review the amendment to Article 9 of the Regulations on Financial Consolidation Bonds for Hubei Province in the 23rd year. Resolution: Refer to the Finance Committee for review. (5) The Economic Committee and Legal System Committee of the Legislative Yuan, together with members Wang Qi, Chen Changheng, Chen Junpu, and Wei Tingsheng, reported on the review of the draft Special Industry Incentive Law. Resolution: The Industry Incentive Law shall be amended and passed according to the review amendment. (6) The Finance Committee and Foreign Affairs Committee of the Legislative Yuan reported on the review of the draft Customs Anti-Smuggling Regulations. Resolution: Refer back to members Lin Bin, Shi Shangkuan, Tao Luqian, Chen Changheng, and Dai Xiujun for review, to be convened by Committee Member Lin. (6th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Current Commentary

A Perspective on Japanese-Puppet Economic Control 25

According to recent reports, the Japanese and puppet authorities have agreed to establish a Japanese-puppet economic co-prosperity treaty with the same effect as a national defense agreement. Under the pretext of developing the national economy of Manchuria, they are actually attempting to intensify the establishment of Japanese control over the puppet state. A telegram from Tokyo on the 5th stated that the original draft of the Japanese Cabinet Resources Bureau on the economic control between Japan and the puppet state is to grant the South Manchuria Railway Company the power to construct the economy of Manchuria. Adopt the form of the puppet state entrusting the company to handle the construction on behalf of the puppet state, and only report to the puppet state afterward. The company's policy is to follow the instructions of the Japanese Cabinet. It can be seen that Japan's summoning of the puppet authorities to Japan this time is actually a preparation in advance. Inferring their psychology, the so-called co-prosperity treaty is nothing more than an attempt to more thoroughly carry out a forceful exploitation of our Northeast people in order to stabilize the economic crisis of Japanese imperialism. But according to our observation, in today's environment, the Japanese have no leisure to carry out economic development in the Northeast. Even the colonial interests they seek may not really be able to compensate for their domestic crisis. To infer the reason, there are several points.

Since Japan seized the four northeastern provinces, all measures have been taken with the establishment of a military base as the primary goal. The policies adopted in recent days are particularly credible. Even in terms of transportation, the completion of the Laha-Bin line has little economic value, and the realization of the Dunhua-Tumen railway is particularly designed to provide great advantages for military transportation. The Japanese use the South Manchuria Railway as the main base for controlling the transportation artery of the Northeast. All the undertakings they carry out are designed to suit the needs and organization of wartime. This is what we are familiar with. Furthermore, to verify it with recent facts, the Japanese have decided to extend the Jinzhou-Chengde railway to Dolon as a preparation for attacking Russia and cutting across Siberia. Their intention to use our East Mongolia as a base for operations against Russia is also obvious. This is one point.

Not only that, Japan's plundering of our Northeast was actually due to fear of the then Northeast authorities' attempt to engage in economic self-defense. When the situation of our side opening up transportation and encircling the South Manchuria Railway was about to be formed, the Japanese ambition was fully exposed. After the loss of the Northeast, the Japanese policy of restricting the economic lifeline of our 30 million compatriots has become more intense. For example, the mutual withdrawal of financial capital from various countries and the horizontal suppression of our country's commercial companies are all reflections of the existence of this policy. Because of this, the capital commodities in various parts of the Northeast are currently under the control of Japanese forces throughout the year. The hard work of the people in the Northeast is only to add huge profits to Japanese imperialists. This trend not only cannot make the economic power of the people in the Northeast gradually become strong, but it is enough to cause the opposition and disputes between Japan's domestic financial capital and the colonial forces in the Northeast. The form of the dispute may be a secret struggle between warlords and financial capitalists, or an open competition between the internal systems of financial capitalists. Regardless of who wins or loses, it has nothing to do with ordinary Japanese people. This is another point.

Therefore, judging from the current situation, Japan's attempt to reorganize its lineup of economic aggression against Manchuria and conclude the Japanese-puppet economic co-prosperity treaty can only be said to be due to its urgent military needs and is not enough to say that it will stabilize its domestic crisis. How can our 33 million compatriots in the four northeastern provinces get even the slightest benefit from it? What is most painful is that with the difficult situation of our Northeast compatriots, there is no way to fill the Japanese's infinite desires even in peacetime. Furthermore, after the implementation of the Japanese strategy of controlling the economy, they will use military requisitioning methods to extract every bit of bone marrow. Can there be any living beings left?

(Tokyo) After the resignation of Army Minister Araki, the zaibatsu's pursuit of the military has become more urgent. Not only did they regain the supervisory rights of the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) in the Diet and smash the Mantetsu reorganization plan of the Kwantung Army's special affairs department, but now they have gone a step further, forcing the military to reform the organization of the Kwantung Army and reduce the Kwantung Army's special affairs department, giving it a final blow. It is reported that Army Minister Hayashi has also agreed and will implement the reform plan during the regular transfer period in mid-July this summer. It is said that the internal details are as follows:

(1) The zaibatsu advocated abolishing the special affairs department, but the internal situation of the military is very complicated. If it is abolished, it will be attacked by the Araki faction, and it will be very difficult to control the military. Therefore, a compromise is taken, only reducing its organization and preventing military personnel from participating in various industrial organizations.

(2) The special affairs department currently has five departments: finance and finance department, transportation department, agriculture and forestry department, industry and mining department, and legal department. Over the past two years, it has decided on concrete plans for construction in Manchuria and its survey materials. Although it has not been able to complete its thorough investigation, there is little left. Therefore, the five departments still exist, but the departments and personnel will be reduced by half, so that the department is sufficient to complete its residual tasks but not enough to control the various industries.

(3) The head of the special affairs department is currently the chief of staff of the Kwantung Army. The zaibatsu had advocated that it be selected by civilian officials, but its organization has been reduced and its duties have been changed to passive. Even if military officers hold this position concurrently, no problems will arise. The zaibatsu will no longer fight on this point and will let the military decide on its own.

(4) Strictly prevent special affairs department members who are registered as military personnel from participating in various industrial organizations.

(5) This reform will be implemented from July 1.

The above-mentioned outline of the reform plan is currently being drafted by the General Staff Headquarters and the Military Affairs Bureau of the Army Ministry. If the Araki faction does not obstruct it, it can be implemented. (China United Press, 6th)

China United Press Tokyo Dispatch, March 30. The Japanese cabinet held a cabinet meeting to review its policy towards Manchuria. This case has caused problems in the Diet and will also be discussed with the puppet Cheng and Hsi about the basic plan for specific measures, so it has attracted attention from all parties. Because its content is easy to cause international discrimination, the Japanese government strictly maintains secrecy. According to the content reported by the Eastern News, it is briefly described as follows: 1. The economic and industrial policy towards Manchuria should be based on Mantetsu and implement the Japanese policy. Therefore, it is necessary to first determine the fundamental national policy for economic and industrial construction, and then decide how to reorganize the Mantetsu company.

2. Resolve the customs issue between Japan and Manchuria and implement economic control between Japan and Manchuria.

3. Expand the organization of Mantetsu and improve its content so that Mantetsu has the strength to control the entire economy of Manchuria.

4. The puppet state railways that Mantetsu is entrusted to operate must be expanded internally and reformed its operating methods as soon as possible from the perspective of national defense, transportation, and industrial needs.

5. The businesses of Mantetsu company other than railways must be separated from Mantetsu company and independently, inducing domestic capitalists to invest freely.

6. The administrative rights of Mantetsu's affiliated land will be transferred from Mantetsu to the Kwantung Office to govern.

7. The Kwantung Office will newly establish a Mantetsu supervisor to supervise all the facilities of Mantetsu, but this facility must be approved by the Privy Council.

8. Even the basic industries belonging to national defense and transportation are not subject to the direct control of the Kwantung Army and are generally under the jurisdiction and management of the Mantetsu company.

This case is the outline of the new policy towards Manchuria drafted by the Cabinet Resources Bureau based on the opinions of the Kwantung Army and Mantetsu, standing in the position of the zaibatsu. The military is very dissatisfied with this case and expressed its opinions after the cabinet meeting as follows:

1. The policy towards Manchuria should recognize Manchuria as an independent country and stand on an equal footing with Japan, and adopt a principle of equal distribution of benefits.

2. The Resources Bureau's plan wants to make Mantetsu's affiliated companies independent to facilitate capital investment and provide necessary subsidies from the Japanese government. This shows that Japan wants to compete with Manchuria for benefits and absorb all the benefits from Manchuria. As a result, it will inevitably stimulate the emerging forces in Manchuria and create an opposing consciousness towards Japan.

3. Russia believes that Japan's policy towards Manchuria wants to monopolize Manchuria politically and economically, and uses this to propagate to the people of Manchuria. As a result, Japan itself proves that its propaganda is true, which is unfavorable to Japan.

4. The Resources Bureau's case is not based on this kind of unthorough foundation and does not seek the common prosperity of the two countries. Therefore, to seek the coexistence and common prosperity of the two countries, a merger principle should be adopted, a trust organization should be adopted, and surgery should be performed on the Mantetsu company, otherwise it will be difficult to achieve the permanent economic control of the two countries.

The military's opinions are like this and they are very dissatisfied with this case. After Army Minister Hayashi visits the elder, he may have expressed it earnestly, but the military is no longer willing to take domestic reform measures, and the leadership has gradually returned to the zaibatsu, and the case will not undergo major changes.

China United Press Siam Correspondence. The headquarters received a letter yesterday from an important overseas Chinese merchant in Bangkok, saying that Siam is the birthplace of overseas Chinese, so the overseas Chinese who engage in commerce, industry, and various other industries in Siam are also more numerous than in other places overseas. Moreover, in terms of the friendship between the two countries, it has always been harmonious. In terms of interests, the economies and politics of China and Siam have a relationship of mutual dependence. However, in recent years, Siam's political unrest has occurred from time to time, and the economy has also been in distress, which has involved many overseas Chinese. For example, the promulgation of import regulations and education regulations has in fact been unfavorable to overseas Chinese in many ways, and the impact on the relations between the two countries is also very great. In addition, the Japanese are eager to plot against Siam, especially regarding the overseas Chinese as a thorn in their side, and thus fueling the flames. Therefore, the position of overseas Chinese in Siam is indeed in danger. In February, the Siamese government held a cremation ceremony for the fallen soldiers who suppressed the rebellion in the Royal Field. A Japanese warship happened to arrive in Siam on the 16th and participated in the ceremony. On the 18th, it hosted a banquet for the Siamese military and political authorities, and then invited people from all walks of life in Siam to visit, nominally to strengthen friendly relations, but in fact to exaggerate the matter to boast about the power of the Japanese navy, which is nothing less than a demonstration. Afterwards, the personnel of the Japanese embassy had many secret talks with the Siamese authorities. It is heard that as a result, Japan will manufacture four cruisers for Siam, each priced at 200,000 Japanese yen. As for why the pricing is so low, it is actually because there is another secret agreement between the two parties. It was also rumored that Japan had obtained a promise from the Siamese government to build a canal at the border between Siam and England, running through the Malay Peninsula, as a new base for Japan's military and commercial activities in the South Seas, and to confront Singapore. This is not without reason. Recently, Japanese small merchants have penetrated deep into the interior of Siam, especially those scattered throughout the areas bordering England and Siam. Along the coast, there are Japanese fishing boats coming and going like shuttles. In normal times, this commercial network can be used to promote the sale of Japanese goods. Once an incident occurs, it will have other uses. Moreover, the political unrest that Siam has accumulated is still deeply latent. If it breaks out again, it will inevitably give the Japanese an opportunity to exploit it. When the world crisis of 1936 breaks out, the Siamese issue may be the fuse for an armed conflict between England and Japan. In addition, the Japanese have widely spread slogans of Japanese-Siamese friendship among the Siamese people. Previously, they published advertisements in the Siamese newspapers, attracting Siamese people to visit Japan. The cost is particularly low. The Japanese side will cover all the costs of ship fares, train fares, food, and accommodation for each person. The sightseeing period is about two months, but the cost is only about 300 baht, in order to arouse the goodwill of the Siamese. This is the same as the so-called "Japan-Manchuria friendship" and "Japan-China friendship". As for the commercial development of the Japanese in Siam, it is giving overseas Chinese a great blow, and since there is no formal commercial treaty between our country and Siam, it is even easier to be squeezed out by the Japanese. In short, the position of overseas Chinese in Siam is quite dangerous at present. If we do not take urgent rescue measures, the future is very worrying.

Arms Embargo Export Case 41

Roosevelt's Attitude Unfathomable

Treating Both Belligerents Equally

Tendency to Accept Senate Amendment

(Washington) U.S. President Roosevelt hoped that Congress would grant him the privilege of prohibiting the export of armaments a year ago. Now, the opinions of the House and Senate on the issue of prohibiting the export of armaments are very different. Therefore, the President's hope for this matter is largely unfathomable. When President Roosevelt took office, the situation in the Far East and South America was tense. Therefore, the President's request for this privilege was nothing more than for the sake of world peace. If the President once had the power to prohibit the export of armaments, then the President's position would be sufficient to allow the United States to collude with the powers to stop the export of armaments that endanger world peace from any country. The President's advisors declared before the Congressional Committee that all governments have the power to embargo the export of armaments. The U.S. government, in order to take consistent action with various countries to seek world peace, also asks Congress to grant it the same power. The House and Senate have already passed the "Bill to Grant the President the Privilege of Prohibiting the Export of Armaments", and the President also firmly believes that Congress will grant him broad powers on this matter. However, in the eyes of the President's advisors, only one of the bills passed by the two houses is barely satisfactory. According to the bill passed by the House, the President has the power to cooperate with other countries to prohibit the transportation of armaments to belligerent countries. However, the Senate added an amendment to the House's bill, which stated that when exercising the power to prohibit the export of armaments, all belligerent countries should be treated equally, without any favoritism. According to this amendment, even if the United States alone or in cooperation with other countries is willing to declare a prohibition on the export of armaments to belligerent countries, it will not be able to do so. It is said that the President has two steps to take on this case. One is to accept the Senate's amendment, and the other is to strive for the Senate to independently pass the House's bill. If the President takes the latter, he will encounter more difficulties, because the minority senators who oppose the case have a way to temporarily shelve the case, and the Congressional agenda is very tight, and the case may even be permanently delayed by the Senate. If the President takes the former, it will inevitably show the government's surrender, but the President and his advisors may think that the sacrifice of fighting for this power is not worth the loss, and decide to accept the Senate's amendment to console themselves. (Reuters, 5th)

US Halts Financial Aid to Debtor Nations 42

Congress Passes Important Bill

Britain Expresses Dissatisfaction at Receiving the Same Treatment

(Washington) Senator Johnson's bill to impose financial blockade on countries that have not paid their war debts was passed by the Senate and the House of Representatives on January 10th and April 4th respectively. This law stipulates that countries indebted to the US, whether they are in complete arrears or only partially in arrears, will no longer be allowed to issue national bonds in the US market. After the passage of this bill, there has been much debate in political circles here about its scope of application. For example, some countries, including Britain, have repaid part of their war debts that have come due in the past to show that they are not repudiating the debt. It is questionable whether the Johnson law applies to these countries. Some say that when Britain and some other countries repaid part of their war debts on June 15, 1933, and December 15, Roosevelt wrote back to the governments of those countries, saying that the US government did not regard the partial repayment of war debts by those countries as a breach of contract. However, Senator Johnson, the drafter of the new law, said, "The financial blockade applies to countries that are partially in arrears as well as countries that are completely in arrears. The wording is very clear, and Britain is included." The State Department was unable to provide an accurate interpretation of the new law today. As for the British Embassy, it said that Britain had repaid part of the debt to show that Britain had the sincerity to acknowledge the debt, and the US had repeatedly acknowledged this in official documents to the British government, so the Johnson law should not apply to Britain. (Havas, 5th)

(London) The bill proposed by US Senator Johnson to stop financial assistance to foreign governments that have not paid their overdue war debts has been passed by both houses of Congress and is only awaiting Roosevelt's promulgation to take effect. The fact that this bill treats Britain the same as other countries that have not repaid their debts is extremely displeasing to all sectors of British society. Official circles are waiting for the law to be implemented before deciding on a course of action. British public opinion believes that the reason why the US Congress is so strict with Britain is because Britain's budget surplus for the previous year was more than 31 million pounds. Americans psychologically believe that since the British treasury is rich, why not repay the US debt? They do not know that the reason why the British Treasury has not fully repaid the war debts that have come due is not due to a lack of funds, but for another reason. On the one hand, the US demands that all countries repay their war debts, and on the other hand, it strictly closes the US market, preventing foreign goods from entering. How can such a method allow international trade to flow freely? This is the reason why Britain is unwilling to fully repay its war debts. As for prohibiting European countries from borrowing money from the US again, this is not taken seriously here, because the London market is full of capital and is worried about not being able to lend it out. (Havas, 5th)

The Crux of US-Russia Debt Negotiations 43

Lies in Russia's Desire to Avoid Acknowledging Old Debts

US Export-Import Bank Suspends Activities

(Washington) The government had established an Export-Import Bank to handle US trade issues with Soviet Russia. The bank's activities have now been suspended. According to a statement from the State Department, US Ambassador Bullitt is in Moscow discussing with the Soviet authorities the issue of old Russian debts to the US. The suspension of the Export-Import Bank is intended to facilitate the early success of these negotiations. US Ambassador to Russia Bullitt has submitted several plans for resolving the debt issue to Soviet Foreign Commissar Litvinov. Bullitt recently reported to the State Department that the debt issue has been submitted to Stalin for review. The main difficulty in resolving the US-Russia debt issue is that the US demands that the Soviet Union pay a total sum, and then the US government will distribute it to the American people who hold bonds from the Tsarist era and the Kerensky era after the revolution. As for the Soviet Union, it is extremely cautious and wants to avoid any action that could be interpreted as directly or indirectly acknowledging the Tsarist debts. However, the board of directors of the US Export-Import Bank has passed a resolution stating that "the board believes that if the Soviet government does not propose an acceptable solution to the debt owed to the US, the US will not be able to lend money to the Soviet Union."

(Havas, 5th)

This revenue will be used mainly for the aftercare fund for veterans. According to congressional sources, the chances of this bill are very good. It has already received the approval of the Design Subcommittee after its meeting. The bill was proposed by House Representative William Shennie, who has investigated the lotteries of China, Belgium, Spain, Argentina, and other Latin American countries, and believes that they have achieved good results, so he decided to adopt them. (National Telegram, 6th)

Labor Unrest in the United States Continues 46

More than 20,000 miners in Fallman and Lockan, Carsten City, Virginia, US, have gone on strike due to disputes with mining companies over demands to comply with the industry regulations set by the Reconstruction Administration, implement a seven-hour workday, and increase wages. In Birmingham, Alabama, coal mining companies have ordered all bituminous coal mines in Alabama to oppose industry regulations that reduce work and increase wages, and they have all been closed. As a result, 15,000 workers have stopped working. The companies have also issued statements in newspapers urging the public and the majority of mine owners to help them resist industry regulations. (Havas, 5th)

(Washington) Although there are signs of renewed labor unrest in the automotive industry, the situation is now easing, as the Federal Automobile Industry Labor Bureau announced today that the strike by 5,000 workers at the Simon Body Company of Wisconsin and the Nash Automobile Factory has now been resolved. (Reuters, 6th)

Verdict in the Assassination of Romanian Premier Duca Finalized 49

Three Principal Offenders Sentenced to Life Imprisonment, the Rest Released

Greatly Exceeding the Government's Expectations

The Determination to Eliminate the Iron Guard Suffers a Blow

Seventy-three members of the Iron Guard, who were arrested in Bucharest for the assassination of Romanian Prime Minister Duca, were sentenced today by the military court of the Second Army Corps. Among them, three were sentenced to life imprisonment. The other two are also students, named Bellesmes and Calinica, all of whom were involved in the conspiracy. This verdict is far from what was expected in Romanian political circles beforehand, because officials all believed that the main offenders could not escape the death penalty, and the accomplices would certainly not be spared. Now, the three main offenders have only been sentenced to life imprisonment, and the accomplices have been acquitted, which is really beyond the expectations of the government authorities, and the government's determination to eliminate the Iron Guard has also suffered a blow. Therefore, such a huge assassination case has ended up with such a result, and it must be said that it is a great failure of the current government. Furthermore, since the verdict was announced, Prime Minister Tartarescu immediately entered the palace to meet with King Carol, so there are rumors outside that the current government has already resigned en masse. However, the Prime Minister later met with reporters to deny this, saying that the current situation is too serious and the current cabinet cannot shirk its responsibilities. Then, its fate will probably be extended to the time when Congress convenes on Friday. It is also reported that the Prime Minister has requested King Carol to implement the "National Security Decree" to crack down on all treasonous acts with severe measures, but whether King Carol will grant his request is still uncertain. (National Telegram, 6th)

Undersea Whisky Binge 51

Diver Drunk as a Skunk

(London) A bizarre news story about a diver occurred here a few days ago, causing everyone who heard it to burst into laughter. A diver (commonly known as a water ghost) was hired to search for sunken cargo in the deep sea. A water boat went to the surface of the sea with him. The diver went down into the water along the sea ladder, and after several hours, there was still no movement, and no goods were raised. Everyone on the boat was extremely anxious. Later, there was a strange movement on the surface of the sea. The people on the boat pulled the sea ladder up and saw that the diver's hands were tightly holding the ladder, and he was extremely drunk. It turned out that he had been drinking whisky in the water 60 feet deep from the surface of the sea, which had caused him to become drunk. When he found a wooden box in the sea, he unexpectedly opened the whisky in the box, causing a large amount of alcohol to flow out. He then drank heavily, resulting in a drunken stupor. (National Telegram, 6th)

International Commercial Telegram

| Special Reuters Market Report, April 6th |

Gold and Silver: London gold price today (6th) was 135 shillings and 1 penny, an increase of 4 and a half pennies from yesterday.

London Silver: Today (6th), the spot price for silver in London was 20 pence, and the futures price was 20 pence and 0.0625, the same as yesterday. American buyers were active in the morning, and European sellers were active. The market closed calmly.

New York Silver: Today (6th), the silver market opened quietly but remained stable, awaiting developments in Washington and other markets. Futures prices, except for the May contract, which rose by two pounds, fell by two to thirteen pounds compared to yesterday's close. Although trading was light after the opening, sentiment remained stable, and traders are currently adopting a wait-and-see approach.

Bombay Silver: The Bombay silver market closed calmly today (6th), rising by one or two annas from yesterday's close. The spot price was 55 rupees and 3 annas.

Exchange Rates

British-American: Today (6th), the London foreign exchange market was very quiet. The opening rate for British-American exchange was $5.15875, an increase of 0.00375 from yesterday's American-British closing rate. It fell by 0.0025 at 11:00 AM to $5.15625 and continued to fall thereafter, but recovered to $5.15125 at 2:00 PM. Additionally, one US dollar was equivalent to 3 shillings and 0.0591 British gold.

British-French: Today (6th), the opening rate for London-Paris exchange was 77.93 francs, a decrease of 3 pounds from yesterday's close. However, it rose by 10 pounds at 11:00 AM to 78.03 francs, then fell by 7 pounds at noon to 77.96 francs. There were no changes at 2:00 PM, remaining 3 pounds higher than this morning's opening.

American-British: New York-London exchange opened today (6th) at 5.15625, an increase of 0.00125 from the previous day's closing price. The second and third trading sessions both had a price of 5.1550. In the fifth session, the price slightly changed to 5.1425. In the sixth session, it recovered to 5.15125.

American-French: New York-Paris exchange opened today (6th) at 6.6050.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: Today (6th), cotton market sentiment was uncertain, and trading was limited. At the opening, bulls engaged in some profit-taking, and there were also sales from Europe and the South, but these were absorbed by fellow traders and Wall Street. Subsequently, due to sales from Liverpool, bulls continued to take profits, and demand for delivery was scarce, leading to further declines.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market was weak at 5:30 PM today (6th) due to widespread profit-taking. The closing was soft, with the price of white Broach cotton for July-August delivery at 198 rupees and 75, a decrease of 2 rupees and 75.

British Cotton: In the Liverpool cotton market today (6th), the price for July delivery was 6.08 at 1:00 PM, a decrease of 1 pound from yesterday.

British Wheat: In the Liverpool wheat market today (6th), the price for July delivery remained unchanged at 4 shillings and 5.5 pence.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market was firm today (6th). The trading price for July-September delivery at noon was 5 and 17/32 pence, an increase of 3/32 pence from yesterday's close.

New York: The rubber market in New York was active and firm today (6th). There were rumors that restriction negotiations in London have reached their final stage, thus the price here increased. Speculators are now showing signs of activity.

Securities

New York: Securities opened mixed today (6th). The general impression is that the Securities Exchange Management Act will be revised repeatedly or temporarily shelved during the current congressional session. However, it is expected that the scope of securities trading will remain narrow pending developments. The market was very sluggish after the opening, but news from brokerage firms was quite optimistic. The majority shares of Zhongxin Securities are now in the hands of powerful individuals. Salt Affairs Conference Concludes 67

Cancellation of Salt Certificates

Planning for Loans for Lianghuai

Implementation of the New Salt Law

(Nanjing) The Salt Affairs Conference convened by the Salt Affairs Administration continued its meeting on the morning of the 6th, chaired by Zhu Tingqi. It was adjourned at 4:00 PM, and Zhu will hold individual discussions with local directors on the 7th. It is reported that the resolutions of the conference were: (1) The abolition of salt certificates. After discussion, detailed measures have been agreed upon and will be implemented in stages. (2) A decision was made to raise a loan of 8 million yuan for Lianghuai, and the repayment method and phased plan have also been largely drafted. (3) Implementation of the New Salt Law. It was decided to centralize the production area, unify transportation and sales, and abolish anti-smuggling measures, to be implemented after achieving unified control. The New Salt Law was drafted in 1930 by Finance Minister Song Ziwen, with the principle of abolishing the salt merchant system and unified sales throughout the country at one time. At that time, salt merchants strongly opposed it, and the Ministry of Finance also had loan relationships with banks, where salt certificates were used as collateral. Once canceled, the salt certificates would be worthless. Therefore, in order to maintain credit, it could not be implemented. It is reported that this time, the Ministry of Finance plans to first repay the loans of Lianghuai and is determined to implement the reform. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has decided to adopt a rotating transportation system for the production and sales of salt in Lianghuai, gradually implementing it with the aim of improving salt transportation, striving for convenience, and reducing private corruption. To address the livelihoods of more than 200,000 sail-transporting boatmen, new salt areas will be opened up in Lianghuai to accommodate some of them, and land will be surveyed in Lianghuai to establish improved local cloth and other factories, so that the boatmen can work in the factories to secure their livelihoods. However, it is stipulated that this will be maintained until the salt workers' children can support themselves. Factory expenses will be covered by part of the revenue from the conversion of salt weight. This will stabilize the livelihoods of the boatmen and also promote the development of industry. (6th Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance is determined to implement the new converted tax rate after the weight conversion of salt. It has instructed Salt Commissioner Zhu Tingqi to participate in the drafting of a response to the two inquiries from the Supervisory Committee member Luo Jiefu, etc. (6th Dispatch)

Seeing the green wheat and yellow rapeseed, a sign of a great harvest year, they all wore expressions of joy. Arriving at the Mausoleum of Emperor Wu of Han around 1:30 PM, the Civil Defense Corps welcomed them with armed formations, displaying a solemn atmosphere and a deep expression of the nation's martial spirit. They still performed the ceremony as before. Then, they paid their respects at the tombs of Wei Qing and Huo Qubing. Huo's tomb had many small mounds and a temple on top. Returning to the province at 5:00 PM, the tomb visit ceremony was simple and solemn, and participants came from all walks of life. It can be truly said to be a national tomb-sweeping. Southern Route Army Bombs and Destroys Bandit Fortifications at Junmenling 92

Recovers Bandit Area of Ling

Guangzhou dispatch: Since the Southern Route Bandit Suppression Army mobilized and pressed into the bandit area, it has been advancing from Chengjiang towards Junmen, having already advanced more than ten miles. The vanguard had a brief encounter with the bandits guarding Junmen. The bandits entrenched in Junmen, led by Ye Jianying, relied on the dangerous terrain and fortifications for cover and were still holding out. The National Army, considering the perilous terrain of Junmen, believed that it would not be easy to destroy the bandit fortifications without the help of the air force. On the 27th of last month, it ordered the air force squadron to carry heavy bombs to bomb the area. After receiving the order, the squadron dispatched planes from Meixian to Junmenling Yuxu to drop bombs, immediately destroying three bandit fortifications. On the 28th, the air force squadron telegraphed, reporting that according to intelligence, the bandit leader Ye Jianying led several thousand remnants to build fortifications at Junmenling, and at 4:00 AM on the 28th, they sent planes to Junmenling Yuxu, dropping two 100-pound bombs and destroying three bandit fortifications, circling the mountain range for an hour before flying back to Meixian.

On the Jiangnan front, since the main force of the First Army advanced towards Anyuan, new defense arrangements have been made. Communist bandits occasionally appeared near Tianxinwei. At the end of last month, more than 1,000 bandits from the pseudo-22nd Division attacked the local anti-communist groups, but they were dispersed. At the same time, Wang Zanbin's troops also discovered more than 100 Red bandits in Qingfeng Mountain and sent Long Zhenyi's regiment to suppress them. They engaged in a fierce battle with the bandits in civilian clothes for two hours, killing more than 40 people and capturing two female bandits. Commander-in-Chief Yu Hanmou, in order to inspect the bandit situation on the front lines, took a plane from the headquarters on the 30th and inspected various bandit areas for a week before returning. He has ordered all frontline units to strictly implement measures to blockade the bandit areas and cut off the bandit areas' food supply. The bandit areas have been facing difficulties in food supply for days.

The bandit area of Ling near Ganzhou is about 80 li from the county seat of Lingdu. Recently, the Communist bandits in the area forced able-bodied men to enlist and forcibly confiscated food, causing resentment among the people. On the 29th of last month, the local people spontaneously revolted, killing several Communist bandit leaders, destroying three pseudo-township governments, and publicly elected popular leaders to request that the Division of the Bull Ridge Defense Army send troops to Ling to garrison. As a result, the officers and soldiers of the Division recovered the bandit area of Ling without firing a single shot. (3rd)

Liu Xiang Orders Troops Not to Impose Levies or Demand Grain 93

Military Food to Be Supplied by the Rear

Chongqing dispatch: Since Liu Xiang was ordered to supervise the suppression of Sichuan bandits, he has recovered most of the bandit areas. Liu received a telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek yesterday, ordering the troops in Sichuan to reduce and exempt grain taxes and miscellaneous levies to alleviate the suffering of the people. After receiving the telegram, Liu immediately forwarded it to the troops, ordering them to comply and not to impose local levies or grain taxes. Liu also telegraphed a reply to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, stating in the original telegram: "Having read your secret telegram from Jiangxi, I am informed that refugees and gentry in northern Sichuan have repeatedly telegraphed complaints about the stationed troops in the disaster area imposing levies and demanding grain. I have ordered all units to strictly warn them not to force levies and to reduce and exempt grain taxes to alleviate the suffering of the people. Your Excellency's compassion for the remaining people and clear statement of military discipline are deeply admired. Since I was ordered to lead the troops this time, I have followed the principle of 30% military and 70% political affairs, as instructed by Your Excellency. I have repeatedly issued strict warnings to the frontline troops to reassure the masses and achieve cooperation between the military and the people. Subsequently, reports from various parties indicate that troops in various places are still imposing levies and demanding grain. After detailed investigation, I found that the reason is that the food in the bandit areas was mostly concentrated and transported away by the Red bandits. After the recovery, the military food was greatly depleted, and sometimes the transportation was not timely, resulting in the aforementioned incidents. I immediately ordered all units not to rely on local supplies for grain and to have all grain and rations supplied by the rear. At the same time, I telegraphed the governments of Hunan and Hubei provinces, requesting them to protect rice merchants, allow them to trade freely, and exempt them from taxes. I also ordered the commanders of various routes to investigate the severity of the disaster in the recovered areas and reduce or exempt grain taxes and miscellaneous levies accordingly for several years, reporting them at any time for verification. I have already exempted Tongnan, Bayi, Dazhao, and Guangxi counties from taxes, aiming to balance the needs of the people and the military. Now that I have received the above instructions, in addition to reiterating the orders to all troops to rest and recuperate the people in accordance with Your Excellency's wishes and not to impose levies again, I respectfully submit this telegram for your consideration. (National News Agency)
