Outline of the Municipal Council's Budget for This Year 129

Submitted for Approval at the Taxpayers' Annual Meeting on April 18

The Public Concession Municipal Council's budget for 1934, i.e., this year, will be submitted for approval at the Taxpayers' Annual Meeting on April 18. The outline of each item is listed below:

Recurrent Expenditure Budget

(A) Under the income item, land tax (collected at 7 per thousand of the valuation) is 6,912,600 yuan, general municipal donation (14 percent of the estimated rent) is 10,648,670 yuan, special municipal donation (12 percent of the estimated rent) is 722,690 yuan, advertising donation is 36,000 yuan, wharf donation is 500,000 yuan, various license fees are 3,077,200 yuan, public property rent is 376,700 yuan, income from public utility and public enterprises is 2,004,000 yuan, miscellaneous income is 126,440 yuan. After deducting the education expenditure budget of 2,263,470 yuan from the above, and adding the surplus from the previous year of 27,400 yuan, the total income is 22,168,230 yuan, and 2,000,000 yuan is withdrawn from the reserve fund, for a total income of 24,168,230 yuan. (B) Under the expenditure item, the business group's expenses are 833,510 yuan, the fire department is 1,134,500 yuan, the police department is 8,700,580 yuan, the prison expenses are 1,335,230 yuan, the health department is 1,118,610 yuan, various hospitals are 584,090 yuan, the health donation is 404,730 yuan, the public works department is 5,690,350 yuan, the music team is 244,050 yuan, the library is 15,310 yuan, the finance department is 1,112,740 yuan, the president and director's office is 512,300 yuan, the legal department is 132,200 yuan, the Chinese language and translation office is 101,990 yuan, the intelligence office is 54,410 yuan, miscellaneous expenses are 1,166,430 yuan, interest and commissions are 865,100 yuan, material costs (excluding those issued at a price) are 120,460 yuan, and the surplus is allocated to the next year is 41,640 yuan, for a total expenditure of 24,168,230 yuan (income and expenditure are balanced).

Temporary Expenditure Budget

(A) Under the income item, the 1934 public bond deposit is 6,993,010 yuan, the sale of surplus land is 3,200,000 yuan, miscellaneous income is 70,000 yuan, and the bonds to be raised are 15,500,000 yuan, for a total income of 25,673,010 yuan. After deducting the temporary education expenditure budget of 1,030,000 yuan, the actual total income is 24,733,010 yuan. (B) Under the expenditure item, the deficit from the previous year is 4,958,570 yuan, the construction of bridges, banks, ditches, and wharves is 737,000 yuan, the land purchase fee is 1,742,910 yuan, various buildings are 3,673,900 yuan, the expansion of roads is 1,700,000 yuan, the purchase of machinery is 166,060 yuan, the pension fund is 370,260 yuan, the repayment of debts and allocation to the fund is 11,362,130 yuan, and the surplus allocated to the next year is 22,180 yuan, for a total expenditure of 24,733,010 yuan (income and expenditure are balanced).

Education Expenditure Budget

(A) Recurrent income, the surplus from the previous year is 75,590 yuan, allocated from the ordinary budget is 2,263,470 yuan, miscellaneous income is 8,240 yuan, for a total income of 2,347,300 yuan. (B) Recurrent expenditure, education administrative expenses are 64,240 yuan, the expenses of various foreign children's schools are 911,640 yuan, the subsidy for foreign schools is 153,850 yuan, the expenses of various Chinese children's schools are 1,028,620 yuan, and the subsidy for Chinese schools is 188,950 yuan, for a total expenditure of 2,347,300 yuan (income and expenditure are balanced). (C) Temporary income, 1,030,000 yuan allocated from the ordinary budget. (D) Temporary expenditure, the land purchase fee is 308,000 yuan, and the construction fee is 722,000 yuan, for a total of 1,030,000 yuan (income and expenditure are balanced).

Accounts for the Previous Year

Regarding the account report for the year 1933, the recurrent income of the ordinary budget for the year was 15,632,867 taels, and the expenditure was 15,613,270 taels, leaving a surplus of 19,597 taels. The tax revenue for the year was 728,263 taels short, of which the shortfall of 466,019 taels in Western-style house donation and the shortfall of 262,915 taels in Chinese-style house donation were the largest. Only the land tax had a surplus of 67,807 taels. However, although the shortfall reached more than 700,000 taels, the result was still a surplus, which was due to the strict savings implemented by all administrative departments. For example, the expenses of business groups, fire departments, police departments, health departments, and public works departments were all below the prescribed amount, and the public works department saved 357,165 taels and the health department saved 113,646 taels, which were the largest. The temporary expenditure budget for the year totaled 24,703,802 taels in income and 22,249,117 taels in expenditure, leaving a deficit of 3,545,375 taels, which has been included in this year's budget to make up for it. At that time, in addition to making a short-term loan of 2 million taels, no additional bonds were raised. Since the sale of the electricity office in 1929, the sale price of 81 million taels was cleared at the end of the previous year. This amount was used to repay 17 public debts, totaling 36,978,144 taels, and to allocate 10,619,640 taels to the debt repayment fund, and to pay 29,616,126 taels for various land purchases and construction costs over the past five years, leaving 3,786,090 taels to be included in the public debt temporary account, which matches the amount of 81 million taels.

Protest by the Guild of Bicycle Manufacturers and Sellers Against Increased Fees 130

Letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce for Negotiation with the Municipal Government

The Shanghai Guild of Bicycle Manufacturers and Sellers, due to the failure of negotiations regarding the increase in bicycle license fees by the Public Works Department, has sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, outlining the reasons for their protest and requesting efforts to overturn the original proposal, as well as forwarding it to the Municipal Government for negotiation. The reasons are quite sufficient, and the original letter is recorded as follows: To the esteemed members of the Chamber, Upon reading the newspaper, we learned that the Public Works Department of the Concession is increasing the bicycle license fee from three yuan to four yuan per year, and also collecting a magnetic tag fee. The motive for this proposal is a suggestion from the French Concession's Bureau of Public Works, requesting the Public Works Department of the International Settlement to do the same. The board of directors has already approved it, and it will be implemented from 1935. At the same time, starting from April 1st of this year, a magnetic tag fee of two jiao per item will be collected. When this news arrived, our guild was extremely shocked. It is unanimously believed that this move by the Public Works Department directly increases the burden on citizens and indirectly affects the business of bicycle merchants. We immediately sent separate letters to the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Shanghai Concession, asking them to find a way to overturn the original proposal. Now we have received a letter from the Association, and the effect is equal to zero. After further discussion among our guild members, we believe that this matter is of utmost importance and we cannot remain silent. We dare to explain it to your esteemed Chamber. The rate of fees, whether increased or decreased, should be based on the general economic situation as a standard. This is true both in ancient and modern times, both in China and abroad. Our city is currently in a period of industrial and commercial depression and economic recession. The general economy has reached an extreme state of hardship. Those who care about the overall situation are dedicated to the recovery plan, but the Public Works Department is proposing to increase fees, pursuing petty gains at the expense of reason. This, based on the current social situation, is absolutely unacceptable and should be protested, this is the first reason. It is found that the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany do not levy bicycle fees at all. France only levies thirteen francs per year, which allows travel throughout the country. Shanghai City originally did not have licenses. Since the Concession's Public Works Department levied fees in 1925, the fees have already been increased once. Moreover, within the Shanghai City area, riders must have at least two licenses to pass. The original fee rate is already higher than any other country. If we consider the price of bicycles, the current ordinary bicycle has a minimum value of less than twenty yuan. The Chinese Concession license fee is five yuan and five jiao per year, which is a rate of 27.5%. In addition, regardless of whether the license is obtained in December or even if the bicycle is ridden for only one day, the fee for the entire year must be paid. Consider the cars on the market worth thousands of yuan. Is the fee rate really 27.5%? If compared, the bicycle fee is even higher than any other vehicle. If it is increased again, can it be said to be fair? This is not in accordance with the principle of equality and should be protested, this is the second reason. According to regulations, the requirement of a bicycle license is originally a method for easy inspection and control, not for the purpose of tax revenue. This is not only admitted by the Public Works Department itself, but also evident in the fact that the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany do not levy fees, and France has a low rate. However, observing the estimates of the Director of Finance of the Public Works Department and the reasons he holds, it is no different from directly admitting that the increase in fees is for the sake of tax revenue. This is a self-contradiction in their words and deeds and should be protested, this is the third reason. As for the two points held by the Public Works Department [due to the convenience of the roads enjoyed by riders and the costs required for police management of traffic], they are difficult to consider as sufficient reasons for increasing fees. Bicycles weigh less than fifty pounds, occupy less than four square feet, travel quickly, and can be placed anywhere. They can be ridden even on rural dirt roads. They do not damage the roads, nor do they obstruct traffic. They do not require designated parking spaces like cars, or the construction of wooden sheds for rickshaws. The cost of police management of traffic is not difficult to imagine. In recent years, the Public Works Department has been increasing road repairs and expansions, as well as adding police traffic control equipment as a result of increasing revenue from cars, etc., and not for the convenience of bicycle riders. This is an undeniable fact. If these two points are used as a reason for increasing fees, then the number of bicycles in the United Kingdom, the United States, and Germany should exceed that of our city by a hundred times. They do not levy fees at all. Do they not need any expenses at all? Or is the management of bicycle traffic in the Shanghai Concession different from other countries? Are the costs required insufficient and must the fees be increased to compensate? The reasons they hold are self-defeating and should be protested, this is the fourth reason. Furthermore, among the more than 30,000 bicycles in our city, 95% are owned by Chinese people, and most of them are from the laboring class. Due to the abnormal development of the current society, soaring rents, and difficulties in making a living, they have no choice but to live in places far from the city. They use bicycles as transportation to and from work in order to save money. These people lack the ability to pay taxes, and the current fee rate is already unbearable. The Public Works Department should give them consideration and find ways to reduce their burden. Now, for vehicles weighing several tons, occupying a large area, easily damaging roads, obstructing traffic, and requiring control and management, there has been no increase in fees. Only the bicycle license fee of one yuan and the magnetic tag fee of two jiao are exacted to exploit the laboring class. Is there anything more unfair in the world than this? This is unequal treatment and should be protested, this is the fifth reason. As for the bicycle merchants in our guild, they pay alarming amounts of money to the Public Works Department. In this time of economic decline and business difficulties, they are already in a precarious situation. If the license fee is actually increased, making it unaffordable for the economically weak laboring class, they will inevitably abandon bicycles and seek other ways to save money. Sales will be hindered, and the reduction of any hope for survival is predictable. For the sake of maintaining the business of our guild, we must strive for this and protest, this is the sixth reason. Moreover, the Public Works Department did not give citizens and related parties sufficient time to consider the increase in bicycle license fees. Once an event is approved by the board of directors, it becomes a set case, leaving no room for protest. It seems that they can take whatever they want. Our tax-paying citizens will not be able to bear the burden. Learning from past mistakes and for the sake of public interest, this must be protested, this is the seventh reason. Furthermore, the Public Works Department currently collects vehicle license fees mostly on a monthly or quarterly basis. For car licenses, if they are discontinued before the expiration date, there is the convenience of refunding the fee. However, bicycle licenses are stipulated to be collected for the entire year. The two methods are extremely unfair. Not only do riders constantly suffer retroactive sacrifices, but our guild also suffers from the lack of sales in autumn and winter, which is extremely painful. In December of the 20th year of the Republic of China, we requested the Chinese Concession authorities to improve this and collect fees on a quarterly basis. Unexpectedly, it was considered that the reasons stated were insufficient to change the basis for collecting fees and were not approved. We believe that business difficulties are even more severe now than in the past, and the various situations of bicycles are as described above, indicating that not only is there no possibility of increasing fees, but there is actually a need for improvement. If we discuss the quarterly method, with the current fee rate of three yuan, on average, those who obtain a license from January 1st to March should still pay three yuan. Those who obtain a license between April and June should deduct one-quarter (i.e., seven jiao and five fen), and actually pay two yuan and two jiao and five fen. The reduction should be made accordingly in autumn and winter. If this is implemented, it will be balanced and avoid the harm of being biased. This is the unanimous proposal of our guild and must be urgently requested. We have always admired the leaders of your esteemed Chamber, who have shown great care. We are sending this special letter to inform you. We sincerely ask you to uphold justice and quickly negotiate with the Public Works Department of the Public Concession and the Bureau of Public Works of the French Concession, based on reason, to not only overturn the original proposal to increase fees but also achieve the goal of collecting the current fee rate on a quarterly basis. We also ask you to forward it to the Shanghai Municipal Government for assistance and send a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers Association of the Shanghai Concession to include it in the agenda of this year's conference for public discussion. Then the citizens will be fortunate, and our guild will be fortunate. We ask that you examine and approve this, and we will all be grateful. We also understand that the members of the Association have a firm attitude and will not stop until the goal of overturning the proposal is achieved.

World Travel Group Passes Through Shanghai 132

Song ZiLiang and His Wife Accompanied

The H company's mail steamer, the "Audacious," carrying a large group of world travelers, arrived at the Songhu port at 3:00 AM yesterday. At 9:00 AM, two small steamers transported some of the passengers from the ship, disembarking at the New Customs Wharf. They then took cars to tour the French Concession, the International Settlement, Zhabei, and other places. They subsequently had lunch at the Astor House Hotel. The ship has a displacement of 20,000 tons, a length of 620 feet, and a width of 72 feet, and is equipped to perfection. This time, it plans to pass through 29 countries and stay briefly in 76 ports, allowing passengers to disembark and tour, completing the entire journey in 137 days. It will leave Songhu this morning at 1:00 AM and head to Korea, passing through Japan, Hawaii, California, the Panama Canal, Cuba, and reaching New York, before returning to Europe. Among the Chinese who joined the ship is Mr. Song Ziliang. Before the ship arrived in Shanghai, Mr. Song repeatedly went to the H company to inquire about the itinerary and destinations of the Lisaroad steamer. According to a confirmed message from the company yesterday, Mr. Song and his wife have changed their itinerary and have traveled from Shanghai to Japan. They are scheduled to board the ship in Kobe when it arrives, and travel to New York. The passenger seats they will occupy have already been reserved on their behalf, and the Kobe branch has been notified to check.

Commodity Inspection Bureau Specially Approves Export of Colored Tea Leaves 134

Foreign Markets Need This Product

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, which had previously prohibited the export of tea leaves colored by tea merchants for fear of affecting foreign markets, has recently found that foreign markets still need this colored tea. The Bureau specially issued a notice yesterday to lift the ban. The original text reads as follows: "It has been found that the coloring of tea leaves should be prohibited. However, since foreign markets still need it, we are temporarily allowing exports based on the situation. Before the absolute prohibition of colored tea leaves, the colorants used should be as pure as possible to ensure that they have no adverse effects on hygiene. It has been found that experts have recently invented eight kinds of yellow colorants with pure quality, which are superior to the colorants originally used for colored tea. The Shanghai Tea Industry Association has set up a factory to manufacture them and has submitted them to the Bureau for registration with the Ministry. In the future, if tea merchants in various places need to manufacture colored tea, they should use only these improved colorants. This notice is hereby issued for compliance. Bureau Chief Cai Wuji."

New Beer Classification Standards Set by the Public Works Department 135

Manufacturers of white beer (i.e., Berlinne Bloode) in this city recently inquired with the Public Works Department about the type of license they should obtain. According to the Director of Health, this beverage is not classified as alcohol in the United Kingdom and should be classified as a type of non-alcoholic soda. He also suggested that beverages containing less than 3% alcohol should not require an alcohol license. According to the Director of Chemical Testing, this white beer contains 2.62% alcohol and is usually mixed with fruit juice. After discussion by the Police Preparedness Committee, it was proposed that if the beverage contains no more than 2.5% alcohol, it may not be considered alcohol, but the label on the bottle must state that it does not exceed this limit. This case was submitted to the Board of Directors and approved for implementation.

Zhejiang Province Actively Promoting Tourism 139

Establishing Tourism Guidance Bureau

Organizing Tourism Association

Zhejiang Province is known for its scenic spots, so during the spring and autumn holidays, people from all walks of life flock to visit. In recent years, the Zhejiang Provincial Government has spared no effort in building roads, making transportation convenient. Therefore, visitors all praise it. However, recently, a modern destruction group was discovered in Hangzhou, causing visitors to be quite wary. Yesterday, Wang Yingbin, Secretary of Construction of Zhejiang Province, came to Shanghai from Hangzhou. The reporter inquired about this matter. According to him, this kind of behavior is naive and reckless and is not allowed by law. It violates police regulations and can even violate criminal law. It is heard that such groups have also been found in the capital and have been cracked down upon. The Zhejiang Provincial Government and the Hangzhou Municipal Government are also making every effort to crack down, conducting strict investigations. At the same time, the public security personnel will do their best to protect the clothing of the people of Hangzhou and the tourists, so there is absolutely no need to worry about accidents. The reporter then inquired about the Tourism Guidance Bureau. According to the answer, it is currently being established jointly by the Zhejiang Construction Department and the Hangzhou Municipal Government. In the future, it will specialize in managing Zhejiang's scenic spots and guiding tourism. In addition, a racecourse will be established, with internal facilities such as oOLO and golf courses for suburban sports. In order to alleviate the congestion of Hangzhou, a number of acres of private land will be enclosed around the racecourse to build a new village. In addition, there will be the organization of a tourism association, with Chinese and foreign leaders as basic members, aiming to encourage travel, promote suburban games, publicize news of scenic spots in various places, and address ethical issues on roads. The Southeast Transportation Tour will be established around the end of June. At that time, the association will invite people from all walks of life to visit, inviting about 150 people. All the films are donated by Kodak. The roads have been protected by troops designated by Chairman Chiang. The Tianmu Mountain and Huangshan roads are under construction. The Shanghai China Travel Service has surveyed locations in various places to establish hotels and prepare for convenient travel. Therefore, tourists who go there in the future will find it very convenient.

Ferry Collides with and Sinks a Boat in Heavy Fog 140

Thirty-Five Ferry Passengers Rescued

Several Still Missing Crew Members Taken Into Custody

At around 6:00 AM yesterday, a ferry traveling to and from the Zhoujiadu area of Pudong was traveling to the Gaochangmiao area of Nanshi when it collided with a Yitaixing Wharf ferry in the fog and sank. More than 30 people on the ferry fell into the water. Except for 30 or more people who were rescued by the police chief of the water patrol team, the rest are still being recovered. The captain of the Yitaixing ferry has been taken into custody for questioning. The details of this incident are as follows:

Ferry Breaks Regulations for Profit

There are many ferries traveling between the Huangpu River and Pudong every day. For the sake of safety on the Huangpu River, the Municipal Public Works Bureau has strictly stipulated regulations to limit the number of passengers on ferries. Generally, larger boats with a length of 80 feet are allowed to carry a maximum of 20 passengers at a time, while smaller boats are limited to 16 passengers. Overloading for profit is strictly prohibited and will be severely punished. This time, Tang Zuofa's ferry, which travels to and from Zhoujiadu in Pudong and Gaochangmiao in Nanshi, disregarded the Municipal Government's regulations for the sake of petty profit and loaded more than 30 passengers when departing from Pudong. Most of the passengers were farmers from Pudong who came to Shanghai to sell vegetables, carrying heavy baskets that filled the boat.

Collision Due to Heavy Fog

When the ferry reached the middle of the Huangpu River, it was traveling from east to west. A Yitaixing Wharf ferry, carrying more than 100 passengers from the Jianghailou customs wharf, was heading to Pudong, traveling from north to south towards the Zhonghua Wharf. It was approaching the Jiangmian River near Gaochangmiao when it encountered Tang Zuofa's ferry. At this time, there was heavy fog, and the river surface was blurred. Tang's ferry was traveling from east to west, coming out from the side. The Yitaixing ferry did not sound a horn, so neither boat was aware of the other. When the two boats were close, it was too late to avoid each other, resulting in a collision that led to disaster.

Ferry Sinks in the River

Tang Zuofa's ferry was violently struck amidships by the Yitaixing ferry. With a loud crash, the more than 30 passengers on board were greatly frightened. At that time, everyone tried to move aside, causing the weight to become unbalanced. The boat was struck by the ferry and could no longer support itself. In addition, the movement of the people in the boat made it unable to remain level, so it immediately capsized. The ferry sank at that time, and the passengers, boatmen, vegetables, and other items all fell into the river. For a time, cries for help arose on the river surface. The bow of the Yitaixing ferry was undamaged.

Water Police Rescue Passengers

After the incident, the City Public Security Bureau's water patrol team received a report and Deputy Captain Li Chengkui and Inspector Pan Xiutong led a large team of police officers on patrol boats to rush to the scene. They worked with the captains and boatmen of the Yitaixing ferry to recover the passengers and rescue those who had fallen into the water. The water police rescued 35 passengers, including Bao Gongming, Zhou Jinsheng, Xie Lanying, Cao Wushi, Yu Linying, and ferry captain Tang Zuofa and boatman Mao Hanhai, all from Pudong. Since they had all been submerged, they were drenched when rescued. After the water police took them to inquire, they were allowed to return home.

Punishing the Guilty Boatmen

However, several passengers, including Xie Youqi, were not seen after falling into the water and may have drowned. Deputy Captain Li of the water police left several police officers at the scene to wait and recover the bodies, and to investigate the names of the dead. The captain of the Yitaixing ferry, Zhang Changlin, was immediately arrested, along with Tang Zuofa, the owner of the damaged ferry, and taken to the district team for preliminary interrogation. Tang was charged with illegally carrying an excessive number of passengers, and Zhang was charged with being the main culprit of the accident. They were sent to the City Public Security Bureau for questioning.

Four Thousand Tons of Brick Tea Shipped to Russia Today 141

Valued at 1.3 Million Yuan

First Shipment of the Year

Recently, due to the lack of ships arriving in Shanghai from the Soviet Union in January, imports were also scarce. However, the brick tea previously purchased by Russia was still not shipped. Now, it has been loaded from Hankou to Shanghai. The Soviet shipping team in this city specially telegraphed to Japan, ordering the Soviet ship Lozosky, which was emptying its cargo in Kobe, to arrive in port today. It is scheduled to dock at the 26th or 27th river pier to load 4,000 tons of brick tea and transport it to Vladivostok, before being transferred to Russia, valued at 1.3 million yuan, and is the first shipment of Chinese tea to Russia this year.

The Asian Editorial Office's Case of Extorting Ma Zhanshan Concludes 143

Wang Haiqiu Testifies that Zhao Feng Organized the Asian Editorial Office

Tang Shichang Proves the Circumstances of Contacting at the Hotel

| Closing Arguments Concluded, Sentencing Scheduled for the 12th |

Wang Haiqiu, from Liaoning, who previously used the name of the Asian Editorial Office to extort General Ma Zhanshan, the famous anti-Japanese general who had retired to Tianjin, was further tried yesterday by Wang Gangxu, the criminal division chief of the Second Special District District Court, in Criminal Court One. Wang had been released on bail and arrived on time. First, the detective's lawyer presented the circumstances of the investigation during the adjournment and submitted the evidence. Then, the witness Tang Shichang was summoned. According to Tang's testimony, before this case occurred, General Ma Zhanshan received a threatening letter and immediately sent a letter to his friend Chongyuan in Shanghai. Du then entrusted it to Yu to contact the defendants. The location was arranged at the Datong Hotel. When Yu went to the hotel, Wang Haiqiu introduced him to a Mr. Liu. Liu said that he was a colleague under General Ma and had suffered with General Ma in the Northeast for a long time. Because General Ma owed his brothers eight months' pay, the brothers were destitute in Tianjin, some even pulling rickshaws for a living, and were in dire straits. They asked General Ma to find a way to solve their livelihood problems and had three reasons (which were sent to me the next day). Otherwise, they would publish a "Short Biography of General Ma Zhanshan." Yu had many conversations with Wang and others, but Wang always said that there was another person in charge. Later, because the matter could not be resolved, it was dropped. When questioned, defendant Wang Haiqiu stated that a civilian named Zhao Feng, who also used the alias Liu Xianda, came to Shanghai with him in January and rented a house at 613 Route Lafayette. The Asian Editorial Office was organized by Zhao and had nothing to do with him. Zhao has now left Shanghai and gone to another port, and he is unaware of the details. He also hired lawyer Xiang to defend him. Then, detective's lawyer Fei Xizhen presented the case, stating that the defendant Wang Haiqiu had committed the crime of attempted extortion under Article 370 of the Criminal Law and requested that he be investigated according to the law. On the plaintiff's side, lawyer Chao Kun acted as an agent and stated the circumstances of the case. After arguments from both sides, the court announced the conclusion of the arguments and scheduled the sentencing for the morning of the 12th of this month. The defendant remained released on the original bail. The three reasons presented by the defendants are recorded below:

Three Reasons

(1) His subordinates said, "We are all subordinates of General Ma, and we have suffered with General Ma for a long time, risking our lives, until we retreated into Russian territory. We never left him. Later, General Ma was detained in Russia, and his life hung by a thread. We all went to the Russian authorities to argue forcefully, declaring that if General Ma was not restored to freedom, we would be willing to die together. The Russian authorities were greatly moved by the loyalty of his subordinates and released General Ma. General Ma looked at us face to face and said with tears in his eyes (referring to General Ma himself), 'I will live and die with you, and I swear to share my fate with you all.' When we departed from Europe to return to China, General Ma still said generously, 'This time I return to China, if I have food to eat, you all will have food to eat. I will never abandon you halfway.' General Ma expressed his determination to us in this way. Although we suffered greatly on the way, we were still grateful and tearful. We also thought that after returning to China, General Ma's whereabouts would be our guiding star. And with our past minor contributions in the anti-Japanese war in the Northeast, under General Ma's leadership, we would surely have a place to settle down and make a living. So, even though life on the way felt difficult, it was the duty of soldiers to endure hardship, and we never complained even slightly. How could we have imagined that after General Ma returned to China, he would receive special treatment from the central government, not know how to work hard and make achievements, be indecisive, and ultimately isolate himself from the central government? He became fearful and quietly went to Tianjin to make other plans. When his subordinates went to see him, he refused to meet them. Since we cannot return to the Northeast because of the anti-Japanese war, and because of General Ma's political misjudgments, we have no way to serve the central government. We suddenly feel that we have no country to turn to and no home to run to. General Ma has forgotten his oath to share life and death and has ruined the bright future of his subordinates because of his fickleness. Now, some of us have worn-out clothes and exhausted our money, wandering in various cities, while others are selling their sons and daughters to barely survive. The suffering of our situation is hard to describe in words. This is the first thing that General Ma should do for us in terms of humanity and conscience." (2) "General Ma has received millions of dollars in anti-Japanese donations from home and abroad, not to mention the money collected locally. He has never made a specific report to the public about the donations he received. Later, at the request of his subordinates, he made an announcement, vaguely stating that he had received a total of 2.7 million dollars (as evidenced by an official order). But when he reported at the YMCA in Shanghai, he suddenly said that he had only received 1.2 million dollars. In this respect alone, General Ma deceived his subordinates, deceived the public, and deceived the government. He owns a huge fortune, but he is so stingy with his subordinates. The situation is too embarrassing. This is the second thing that General Ma should do for us in terms of humanity and conscience." (3) "This time, General Ma has entrusted certain individuals to mediate, which shows that General Ma has realized that we have been following him for a long time. Publishing a short biography to express our grievances is an act of desperation. If General Ma is willing to understand the situation of his subordinates, we will naturally know when to stop and will not go to extremes. As for why we have not told his real name, it is to leave room for future meetings, to let each other get by. Unless General Ma truly does not realize the situation and truly does not understand, then we will know that General Ma has decided to pursue his own well-being and will not seek a place for his old subordinates who are wandering and displaced. At that time, we will not only have to tell his real name, but we will also have to step forward and show our faces, meet with General Ma with formal procedures, and make a clear announcement in the newspapers, appealing to social groups, party and government military departments, news agencies, and the public for a fair judgment. Therefore, it should be known that our actions are truly a matter of life and death, forced by desperation. This is the third thing that General Ma should do for us in terms of humanity."

A Letter

Also, a letter from the defendants to Ma Zhanshan is recorded below: General Xiufang, may everything be auspicious. I know quite well the matter between the General and the Asian Editorial Office. I dare not remain silent about the dangers. They have all shared hardships with the General and do not want to act too hastily, but the General treats them as strangers. This is truly impossible. People also say, "Treat me like a national scholar, and I will repay you like a national scholar; treat me like an ordinary person, and I will repay you like an ordinary person." Now the General treats people as strangers, how can he make people continue to regard him as sacred? Moreover, people are emotional creatures. If they meet with sincerity, no grievance cannot be resolved. If you treat people harshly and put them in a desperate situation, there will inevitably be a day of outburst. The resentment of poison towards people can never be forgotten by the sufferer. Then, what other option is there except to fight the General for the final victory? Now, seeing that the General has severed all ties of kindness and righteousness, they are actively carrying out the liquidation of donations, the recovery of back pay, and the early publication of a short biography, all at the same time. Under the pressure of riding a tiger, they have no choice but to ignore everything. The General's future downfall and disgrace is as clear as fire. If he still clings to his delusions, the harm will be immediately apparent. I have been with the General for a long time and must offer this final piece of advice. I have said all I can, please think it over.

A Man and Woman Commit Suicide by Poison at the Central Hotel 144

Unable to Marry and Divorce

Resorting to This Desperate Measure Due to Intense Love

At the Central Hotel at the intersection of Guangdong Road and Hubei Road in the Public Concession, a man and a woman arrived at the hotel at around 4:00 PM the day before yesterday and requested a room. The hotel clerk assigned them room number 525. They paid the room fee of two dollars on the spot. The man called himself Zhang Ankang, 30 years old, a local. The woman was named Zhou Qiming, 24 years old. After the tea server brought the tea, Zhang Ankang immediately asked for paper, ink, brush, and inkstone, closed the door, and wrote a letter. After a long time, he finished writing and then went out with the woman. They returned late at night. At around 10:00 AM yesterday morning, the tea server knocked on the door to ask if the room was still needed. There was no response for a long time. The tea servers thought that the two were still asleep. At 12:50 PM, they knocked again, but still no one answered. The tea servers became suspicious and took a key to open the door, but the spring lock was locked. The tea servers tried to enter through the transom and opened the door. They saw a man and a woman in the bed, both pale, with only a faint breath. Beside the pillow was a bottle of sedative pills. They knew they had taken poison and quickly informed the clerk and reported to the police, who rushed the two to Renji Hospital for treatment. After the hospital administered emergency treatment, they regained consciousness. When asked about the reason, they claimed that the man was Zhang Ankang, 32 years old, from Jiangwan, living at 391 Jiangwan Main Street. The woman was Zhou Qiming, 24 years old, from Baoshan, living outside the West Gate of Baoshan. The two had known each other for a long time, but Zhang was already married in an old-fashioned arranged marriage, and their relationship was not good. Zhang had planned to divorce his current wife and marry Zhou, but the parents of both sides were not satisfied, so it did not happen. But he could not bear to part with Zhou. With no way out, they had the idea of being tired of the world and committed suicide by poison together.

Guest Shoots Host After Full Moon Celebration 146

Liao Amao First Gives Gifts Then Borrows Money, Actually For Women

Yuan Genfa Celebrates Son's Birth With Guests, Ultimately Shot

At around 9:00 PM last night, a shooting occurred at the Zhuangyuanlou Restaurant on Xixinqiao Street (i.e., Baliaoqiao Street) in the French Concession. The victim was a gangster who was shot twice and was in critical condition. The details are recorded below:

Marrying and Raising Children 147

Yuan Genfa, from Hangzhou, Zhejiang, is 34 years old and lives in the east wing of 7 Renan Lane, Gero Road (i.e., Songshan Road) in the French Concession. He married the daughter of the famous madam Wang of the Wangji brothel (28 years old). Last year, they had a son named Debao. Yuan was arrested several years ago in connection with the robbery of 46,000 dollars from a bank and sentenced to four and a half years in prison. He was released at the end of last year.

Hosting a Banquet for Guests 148

After Yuan was released, he lived with his wife and mother-in-law in Renan Lane and also worked as a bookkeeper for the Ruihua Brothel in Hongyunfang, Huage Road. He was able to turn over a new leaf. Yesterday was his son Debao's first birthday. Yuan sent out invitations and hosted a large banquet for friends and guests at the Zhuangyuanlou Restaurant at 9-11 Xixinqiao Street on the second floor. The guests were all gathered together, making it quite a grand occasion.

Borrowing Money Under False Pretenses 149

At around 9:30 PM in the evening, the guests began to leave one after another. There were still more than ten people talking on the second floor. At that time, Yuan took the wooden box containing the gift money to the first private room on the third floor to check and sort it out with his wife, Wang. As they were counting the money, a guest named Liao Amao suddenly entered and asked Yuan to borrow 30 dollars. Yuan did not agree to his request. Before he could finish his answer, shots were fired.

Shot and Fallen 150

Seeing that Yuan did not agree, Liao suddenly pulled out a pistol and shot at Yuan. The first bullet hit his right chest. Seeing that the situation was not good, Yuan instinctively raised a wooden bench to resist. Liao then fired three more shots at him. Yuan was hit in the left chest by another bullet and fell to the ground. At the same time, Yuan's wife shouted for help. The murderer, seeing that his goal had been achieved, hurried downstairs and left. When the people on the second floor heard the gunshots, they did not know what had happened at first. When they heard Yuan's wife shouting for help, they rushed upstairs.

Detective Investigation 151

When the people went upstairs, they saw Yuan groaning on the ground. The restaurant's clerk quickly reported to the police by telephone. Chinese and Western detectives arrived together and first sent Yuan to Renji Hospital. Then, they thoroughly investigated the scene, first collecting all the bullet casings. The glass window of the first private room was pierced, and the bullet hit the north-facing whitewashed wall, forming a small hole. The bullet was gone. Two bullets pierced through the floorboards of the second and third floors, reaching the lower-level hall. One bullet damaged a piece of whitewashed wall, and one bullet landed on the corner of a table, forming a small hole. The power of the murderer's pistol can be imagined.

Women's Issue 152

After the detectives finished their investigation, they immediately reported to the police chief and began to investigate. According to those close to Genfa, the murderer and Yuan were good friends and were one of the invited guests. He also gave four dollars as a gift when he came. It is said that Yuan and Liao had a quarrel over a woman's issue, and the motive for the murder may have been laid in advance. However, after Yuan was sent to the hospital, the doctor found that both bullets had hit vital parts. He needed to have an operation to remove the bullets immediately, and there was little hope of survival.

Municipal Authorities Actively Prepare for Pudong Water Supply 153

A Fixed Amount of 300,000 Yuan is Determined to be Jointly Operated by Government and Business

Business Shares Have Been Secured, Government Shares Are Still Being Raised

The Municipal Government believes that Pudong lacks water supply equipment and the residents' needs are urgent, so it has decided to raise funds to create a water supply company. According to responsible personnel of the Public Utilities Bureau, the company will be jointly operated by the government and business, with a capital of 300,000 yuan, which will be raised separately by the two parties. All plans have been generally drafted. The only difficulty is the economic problem. At present, through the efforts of local gentry in Pudong and business leaders in the city, business shares have been largely secured. For government shares, the Municipal Government plans to borrow from the banking community due to revenue shortfalls. The outcome is still unpredictable. In short, this undertaking is urgently needed, and the authorities are determined to plan it carefully, hoping to complete it in a short period of time. The preparatory personnel are Xu Peihuang of the Public Utilities Bureau and Cai Zengji of the Finance Bureau on the official side, and Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Yao Mulian, etc. on the business side.

Public Utilities Bureau Operates Public Buses to Meet Longhua Traffic Needs 154

Traffic between Nanshi and Longhua is extremely important, especially during the beautiful spring, when the peach and plum blossoms near Longhua are vying for beauty, and Shanghai residents are competing to go to offer incense and sightsee. The public buses operated by the Public Utilities Bureau, the first route of which passes through Laoximen and returns to Laoximen, taking Fangxie Road, Zhizaoju Road, and Kangding Road to reach Longhua Town. Since the opening of the service on April 1, the number of passengers has been increasing daily. The vehicles are newly styled, elegantly decorated, comfortable to ride, and cheap to fare. It costs only 48 copper coins for the entire journey from Laoximen to Longhua Town. A bus departs every five minutes, which is convenient for passengers.

Newspaper Association Continues to Sell Newspapers on Beijing-Shanghai Line Passenger Cars 156

Supplementing the Contract Terms for Another Year

The business of selling newspapers on the Beijing-Shanghai line passenger cars was previously contracted by the Shanghai Newspaper Association. The contract expired on February 28 of this year. The association requested to continue the business for another year from March 1 of this year and requested to add a clause to the contract stipulating that if a special accident occurs on the line during the contract period, causing the entire line or a section of passenger cars to stop running, the carrier's vehicle rental fee will be reduced on a daily basis according to the number of stopped cars and mileage. The Vehicle Affairs Office also made a similar request when the association previously renewed the contract for selling newspapers on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line. After several negotiations, referring to the general idea of Article 21 in the contract signed between the two lines and the Dafeng Transit Silver Company for transporting silver, it was revised to state that if war or other circumstances occur during the contract period that obstruct the operation of the entire line of passenger cars, this contract may be suspended until the passenger cars resume operation. The number of days of this suspension may be made up in full after the contract expires. However, this does not apply if only a section of passenger cars on the entire line is stopped for less than three days. If the stoppage exceeds three days, the Railway Bureau may consider the situation and supplement the number of days after the contract expires according to the above method. It is now planned to handle this matter in accordance with the precedent of adding a clause to the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line. The Bureau has approved the implementation, it is said.

Partial Trial Record of the Murder Case of Notorious Robber Li Chunsheng and Others 161

Wang Chengying, a Chinese detective of the Jiading Road Police Station, and detective Yang Xiguang, previously arrested six robbers, including Cao Zhenxi, Li Chunsheng, and Tang Xuyou, for conspiring to rob the Wang family at 5 Donglai Lane, Yangshupu Road, on September 13 of last year, of property worth dozens of dollars. Investigation revealed that Li Chunsheng had committed multiple assassination cases between 1926 and December 1929. Subsequently, more than ten accomplices, including Xia Shaoqiu and Gu Rufang, were arrested and brought to the First Special District Court for repeated questioning, which has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. In the robbery portion of the case, Cao Zhenxi, Xu Debiao, and Du Baoliang were sentenced to imprisonment, while Li Chunsheng, Tang Xuyou, and Yuan Xingfu were found innocent. Yesterday morning, the police presented Li Chunsheng, Xia Shaoqiu, Gu Rufang, Wang Ruiting, and the convicted prisoner Kong Guangfu, and others, to Criminal Court Three. Wang Yaotang, the lawyer of the Public Works Department, stated that the detective in March 1928 (i.e., around 6:00 AM on the 5th day of the second month of the lunar calendar) shot and killed Bao Tongshi, the female head of the Yangzhou textile factory, on Gordon Road. During the rescheduling, the defendants were taken to the scene of the incident to demonstrate how they carried out the crime and admitted it to the police station. It was found that the pistol was taken from Wang Ruiting and given to the two defendants, Li and Xia, to shoot. Confessions of each defendant have been recorded and are hereby submitted for inspection. At that time, she was going out of the factory when she suddenly heard three gunshots. She was first hit in the hand, and the last bullet entered from the back and exited from below the front breast, killing her. His wife had no enemies, and it was heard that she was instigated by the leader of the labor union. The Guo offender has already been sentenced to life imprisonment, etc. However, lawyer Wang Yaotang stated that the two offenders, Guo and Shi, were arrested by the Putuo Road Police Station and sentenced to life imprisonment on November 15, 1929. However, the two offenders did not accuse the defendants of conspiracy when they were identified by the police, so they were not brought into the case. When questioned, the five defendants, Li Chunsheng and others, completely overturned their previous confessions at the police station, making excuses for each other, all claiming that they had nothing to do with it, and asked for judgment. Judge Xiao Fen ordered them to be remanded and rescheduled for further verification.

In this city, on the evening of March 20, the wall of the small Luzon hat store in the Poluo Ball Park was blown down by a hurricane. Wang Jindi, a cobbler, happened to be passing by and was crushed by cement bricks, causing his left kidney to rupture and his injuries to be very serious. It is said that he had suffered from stomach problems for five years. This time, the stomach was affected due to the impact. At around 8:15 AM yesterday morning, a fire suddenly broke out in the cotton ginning room of the Gutiansheng cotton factory in Tanziwan, Zhongshan Road, Zhabei, burning several bales of cotton, with losses estimated at about 2,000 yuan. After various fire brigades rushed to the scene to put out the fire, it was extinguished at around 9:00 AM. Afterwards, because the factory owner Gu Mingfa was not present, the factory employee Li Genfa, 30 years old, from Wuxi, was detained in the Fourth District Branch for temporary custody, pending investigation of the details of the fire.

New Contributions from the Ant Library 167

Publication of the Second Issue of the Library Catalog

In recent years, the surge in commodity prices and the decline in people's livelihoods have affected cultural endeavors, leading to increasing numbers of young people dropping out of school and being unable to afford books. Recognizing this, the Ant Society, guided by its commitment to cultural movement and public service, has opened its entire collection of books in the Ant Library to the public, and adopted a mail-in borrowing and return system to promote accessibility. It has also waived guarantee and handling fees to adapt to the adverse economic conditions, so its reputation has spread throughout the country. Readers have gathered from afar, even from Korea and Sichuan and Yunnan, all considering it a pioneering initiative among the nation's libraries and praising its convenience. The library has been painstakingly managed for three years, and its collection has more than doubled. Recently, it compiled and printed the second issue of its library catalog to contribute to readers everywhere. With this catalog, one can enjoy the right to borrow books unconditionally. Anyone interested in reading can send ten cents in postage stamps to Shanghai Post Office Box No. 2064 or No. 536 Sichuan Road, and the library will send a copy. The library has also entrusted the Modern and Guanghua bookstores to sell it on its behalf, for the convenience of all sectors.

Domestic Zhanghua Woolen Fabrics Sell Well 168

Zhanghua Woolen Textile Company specializes in manufacturing domestic woolen fabrics and serge. The leaders possess new ideas, a broad vision, and a strong will, resulting in continuous reforms and progress. The company breathes life into the domestic goods industry and is highly regarded by the Chinese people. As a result, its business has expanded, and a new branch store has been opened in Nanjing, which will open on the 7th. Shanghai is holding a sale with low prices. Because its goods are selling so well, the factory is working night shifts and has not stopped at all. This phenomenon, while due to the quality of the products, also reflects the patriotic spirit of the customers.

City News

Recent Situation of Sanyu Chicken Farm The tragic reality of rural bankruptcy in China has become increasingly severe in recent years. Efforts by people in and out of the government to rescue the situation have often been criticized for being unrealistic and lacking practical force. Zhang Xiaokuan, a graduate of agricultural studies, has always advocated developing rural sideline industries to revive rural areas. He believes that chicken farming is the most common sideline in Chinese villages and should be improved and developed. Therefore, after the end of the January 28th Shanghai Incident, he established Sanyu Chicken Farm in Maqiao Town in the county. He planned meticulously and managed painstakingly. Although the scale is still relatively rudimentary, the organization is orderly. The farm specializes in raising the world-renowned [Leghorn] egg-laying chickens. The management adopts the latest scientific methods. All eggs sold are carefully selected, white, round, fresh, and reliable. Each egg weighs between 1.7 and 2.4 taels, and its nutritional value is self-evident. The farm also sells fertilized eggs, which are produced by mating strong, excellent, unrelated parent chickens. Experimental results show that the fertilization rate reaches over 85%, the hatching rate reaches over 95%, and the survival rate reaches over 94% (referring to chicks within four weeks). The fully grown chickens are all very large and excellent. It is said that visitors from all walks of life have expressed satisfaction and are happy to purchase them. Currently, the farm is sparing no effort to improve its equipment and management to achieve perfection, in order to live up to the expectations of the community.

Opening of Hongxiang Company Branch Hongxiang Company has recently moved its branch to a new location because the original building was insufficient. The renovations have been completed, and the official opening is scheduled for the 8th of this month. Modern overcoats are priced at 27 to 45 yuan each. Wedding dresses and after-wedding attire are available for rent on the first floor for 10 yuan per set. Special overcoats and evening dresses on the second floor will be discounted in a joint sale with the main branch for 21 days starting from the 8th. The latest spring fashions are all-inclusive. Customers from all walks of life are welcome to visit and make their selections.

Sanlun Brand Goods Sell Briskly The Sanlun brand of woolen and cotton knitted swimsuits, pure silk stockings, and mercerized cotton socks produced by Lianhua Woolen Mill in Hele Lane, North Henan Road, have been around for ten years. Over the years, they have been continuously improved. The styles are in line with the times, and the materials are superior. They are no less than foreign goods. Therefore, the factory has recently received a large number of orders from domestic and Southeast Asian customers, and the supply is struggling to meet the demand. This is a good phenomenon for the domestic goods industry. The factory, in view of the fact that the imperialists in the Dutch East Indies (Java) have drastically increased import taxes, has decided to make special sacrifices this year to reclaim the benefits and glory for the domestic goods industry.

Dongya Photo Spring Giveaway Opposite Xiaocai Chang, Baxianqiao, French Concession, Dongya Art Photography Company, in view of the bright spring scenery and the time for photography, is holding a spring giveaway for free enlargements for ten days. The crowds have been exceptionally large, and they have been unable to accommodate everyone. Dongya is a pioneer in offering free enlargements in Shanghai's photography industry. Its work has always been unique, and a photo for one yuan includes a 10-inch enlargement, while a photo for 1.5 yuan includes a 12-inch enlargement, which is especially appreciated by Shanghai women. The attached express development and printing department can have your items ready the same day, which is unique in Shanghai. Recently, due to the spring holidays, the number of items submitted for development and printing by people from all walks of life has been overwhelming, but the company is still able to handle it with ease. The thoughtfulness of the service is evident here.

Gaochengxing Business Flourishes Gaochengxing Wine Shop, located on Fourth Ma Road, East of Shilu Road, has been established for nearly 20 years and has a strong capital base. It is the only famous Shaoxing wine shop in Shanghai. Its fine wines, such as Chennian Taihao Huadiao, Yuannian Yixiang, Zhuyeqing, and Jingzhuang, are all produced in its own factories in Yue and have been famous for many years. The business is thriving. Taihao Huadiao is priced at 50 cents per bottle, and it has multiple bicycles for prompt delivery. The shop is a three-story Western-style building. The second floor and the floor below are connected and clean, with spacious seating. There are elegant private rooms on the third floor, and the service is attentive, which is convenient for customers. Now that the Spring Festival is approaching, the store is bustling with activity, and the sales of Taihao Huadiao and Chennian Jingzhuang are particularly strong.

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the northeastern part of China and Shandong are cloudy with rain and cyclones due to a low pressure passing through and moving east. The Yangtze River basin and this area are cloudy and clear, with fog in the morning and indeterminate wind direction. The coastal area south of Ma'an Island is cloudy with rain and northeasterly winds. Respectfully informing benevolent individuals who are devoted to recommending the deceased and prolonging life

This time, we respectfully invite the Panchen Lama to West Lake to practice the Kalachakra Tantra Dharma Assembly in order to eliminate disasters in our country and pray for world peace. We will take this opportunity to also ask the Panchen Lama to practice two kinds of Dharma incidentally, one is the Dharma of Recommending the Deceased, in order to recommend our ancestors and all lonely souls, so that they may be reborn in the Pure Land early, and the other is the Dharma of Prolonging Life, in order to eliminate the disasters of our living parents and ourselves, so that life can be extended. These two Dharma are very important, and we must practice them once a year. However, the previous practices did not have much merit, because although the Dharma is the same, the people who practice the Dharma are different, and the merit is also different. The Panchen Lama is the Dharma King of Tibet and also the National Teacher of China. Tibetans call him the incarnation of Amitabha Buddha. This time, he recites sutras, chants mantras, and orients for us, because his foundation, learning, and cultivation are all very great, so the merit of practicing the Dharma is naturally very great, which is thousands of times higher than our usual practice of asking people to practice Dharma. This opportunity is truly rare and also because we have this karma. Reading Q&A 176

Reading Guidance on Marriage Issues Expressed in "Little Ten Years"

From reading the book, I have a question that I would like to ask. Although it is not about the book itself, this question arose from reading the book, so I am bringing it up. I am a person who has suffered from this question for a long time, and I think there must be many young people who have the same problem as me, so I hope you can give a detailed answer.

The reason is this: In the second volume of Mr. Ye Yongzhen's "Little Ten Years," he wrote about how he bravely sacrificed his old-fashioned wife. At that time, his mentality was very intense. He would rather leave his family, his beloved mother, and his wife with whom he had shared a bed for several days, and finally left to meet his lover.

This touched me greatly, but what confuses me most is that someone wrote a comment in the book (this book is from the library): "Bah! You are brave enough to break this dark, buying-and-selling marriage, but what about the other party, your wife with whom you have already shared a bed?" Behind this sentence, another person spoke out for the wronged: "Bullshit! You compromiser! Should he abandon his own happiness to succumb to the darkness? A centrist!" The theoretical struggle between these two gentlemen really confused me, because I am also in an environment like Mr. Ye, but I finally became a centrist.

Because I usually care a lot about this marriage issue, I have collected the opinions of the above two parties and explained them as follows: But I don't know which one is right?

The brave ones believe that new young people should never tolerate fighting with the environment, especially in marriage. The old-fashioned, buying-and-selling marriage is unacceptable. An unfamiliar wife with no love should never live with her. Regardless of stubborn parents or a feudal society, they should never compromise.

The centrists, on the other hand, believe that today's society has not yet advanced to another new stage. Those who are born in this unfortunate stage of transition, although they should promote society to move towards a new stage, can still be patient in marriage. The reason is that in this capitalist society, everything is commodified, even women. Therefore, most people who marry for love will end up losing love and divorcing, especially in this city where money and desires flow rampant. Which modern woman will have sincere love? It is better to compromise and marry a woman from the countryside, and maybe you can live a very sweet married life. There are many young people with this mentality. When I was in junior high school, two-thirds of the students in my grade were married, completely in the old style. Some were very good, and some were bad. I am one of them.

Sir, these two completely different arguments are very confusing to me, and maybe to many other young people too!

Marriage is a lifelong event. Although I have already made a mistake, I hope to get a correct answer so that future young people will not follow in my footsteps. (Letter from Liu Yingyun, Jinan)

Cao Yunxiang to Attend the Meeting in Place of Wang Zhengting

Sports Association Cables Reply to Philippine Overseas Chinese, Attitude is Resolute

Representatives of the Island to Arrive in Shanghai Tomorrow

The Round Table Conference of China, the Philippines, and Japan, which is about to be held on the 9th, has now been officially confirmed. Yesterday, an official from the Chinese Sports Association told reporters that Dr. Wang Zhengting has cabled Shanghai, stating that he is busy with affairs in Ping and cannot spare the time to travel south. Our side has three representatives, Wang Zhengting, Hao Gengsheng, and Shen Siliang. Now that Wang is unable to attend, it has been decided that Cao Yunxiang, the former president of Tsinghua University, will attend in Wang's place, and his agreement has been obtained. The meeting place was originally planned to be at the Palace Hotel, but it must be decided after consultation among the representatives of the three countries. Japanese representatives Yamamoto and Matsuzawa have arrived in Shanghai, but they have not yet met with our association. The Philippine representatives will arrive on the 8th. Our association has repeatedly expressed the content of the meeting, adhering to the principle of not discussing with puppets and not associating with puppets. Overseas Chinese have also sent cables of warning, their enthusiasm is commendable. The Japanese are cunning and treacherous, trying to cover up the eyes and ears of the world with one hand, forcing us to indirectly acknowledge them. It is impossible to endure humiliation and seek perfection. If they insist on bringing it up, or if the Philippine side is deceived by them and allows the puppet Manchukuo to participate in an individual capacity, then our side is determined to withdraw. According to Mr. Matsuzawa, the Japanese representative, his arrival in Shanghai is purely to assist Yamamoto in attending the Round Table Conference. How to deal with the situation if China does not allow the puppet state to participate will depend on Dr. Yamamoto's decision. However, according to reporters' inquiries, the Japanese attitude is very strong, and they have the momentum of achieving their goals. If our side is determined not to lose its rights and humiliate the country, then the future of this Far Eastern Games seems bleak.

Letter to the Authorities from Two Track and Field Teams

Willing to be a Backing, Do Not Harm the National Prestige

To Mr. Wang Zhengting, Mr. Hao Gengsheng, Mr. Shen Siliang, and the sports authorities: Japan is妄thinking of using sports to aid its political aggression, instigating the puppet state to participate in the Far Eastern Games, hoping to create an equal position between the puppet state and us, so that our country tacitly acknowledges the puppet state, which is a hint, and can confuse the world's perceptions. This is what is called "Sima Zhao's heart is known to everyone on the road." Recently, the Japanese have used all kinds of cunning tricks, one after another, and sports envoys have been traveling continuously. They falsely claim that there is a call for a round table conference, and falsely claim that a round table conference has been realized. At the same time, a senior official of the Ministry of Education suddenly made a statement allowing individual performances by the puppet state, although Mr. Shen Siliang subsequently expressed that the issue of the puppet state's participation would not be discussed. However, the public is panicked, and they are telling each other in alarm, running around to report, and they cannot completely dispel the doubts of the Chinese people. What is the round table conference discussing? What is the scope? Are there representatives from the puppet state participating? Why are the venue and date of the meeting kept strictly secret? Is there anything unmentionable hidden in it? These are all things that the whole country is watching closely and waiting for the sports authorities to explain clearly. The Japanese say, "Politics and sports are two completely separate things. Do not harm sports with politics." Their words are certainly enough to decorate, but we are fortunate not to fall into their trap. Politics restricts sports, and the impact is small. Sports restricts politics, and the impact is great. We would rather sports be sacrificed because of politics than politics be sacrificed because of sports. Understand this, and our country should put attending the Far Eastern Games out of its mind and not be softened by political pressure. If not, or if the puppet state is allowed to participate formally or substantially, it would be tantamount to tacitly acknowledging the establishment of the puppet state in disguise. One word can ruin a country, and the crime is unforgivable. Is the sports cause that the whole country enthusiastically promotes and supports for this purpose? In short, at the Far Eastern Games, there is the puppet state without us, and there is us without the puppet state. This is a matter of course and should not be hesitated. If there is any hesitation, it will inevitably lead to eternal regret. Fortunately, you gentlemen firmly advocate宁sacrificing sports rather than sacrificing the country. The members of the two teams pledge to be a backing. We wish you good health. The Beijing China Track and Field Team and the Shanghai Baihong Track and Field Team, April 6th.

Li Gongying Wins the Title of Shanghai Billiards King Again 185

Wins This Year's A Group Championship Again

Mrs. Beller Presents the Award at the Meeting

Our country's billiards king, Li Gongying, defeated Kang Pusi with 2,000 points to 1,126 points in four games yesterday and the day before, winning this year's Shanghai Amateur Billiards Association A Group Championship again. The honor of Shanghai Billiards King belongs to Mr. Li again. The competition ended at 11 PM last night. President Beller gave a speech and reported the results of various competitions held by the association in 1934. (1) The Chinese team won the Sino-British international match (team members: Li Gongying, Shen Lince, Liu Fuzong, Xu Shizhang, Hu Changyuan). (2) Champions of each group: (A Group) Li Gongying, (B Group) Clark, (C Group) Lin Baohua. Mrs. Beller then presented the awards and the meeting adjourned.

Li's Victory Process 186

Li Gongying's billiards and Li Huitang's football are equally famous in Shanghai. This time, the professional master Willie Smith came to Shanghai, and Mr. Li gained a lot of experience, and his performance became more and more miraculous. In this competition, he first defeated Su Shi, then lost to Marx, then defeated Sha Xuem, and finally defeated Kang Pusi. Among the above battles, the final was the most exciting, and the second day yesterday was especially tense. In the daytime game, 1,000 points, the huge numbers were 45, 36, 29, 21, 56, 35, 20, 106. Japanese Davis Cup Main Player Sato Commits Suicide by Jumping into the Sea 189

Caused by Extreme Neurasthenia

Sato's Funeral to be Held by the Tennis Association

Fukuda Added to the European Team, Miki Appointed Captain

(Japanese United News Agency, Tokyo Fast Electric, 6th) According to a telegram received by the Japanese Tennis Association, Sato Jiro, a Japanese Davis Cup tennis player who is currently on his way to Europe, committed suicide by jumping into the sea from the Hakone Maru in the Strait of Malaga on the evening of the 5th. (Note) Sato graduated from Waseda University and won the national singles championship in 1930. In 1931, he participated in the Davis Cup tennis war. This year, he was again appointed as a Davis Cup player representing Japan. He is 25 years old. His backhand is excellent, and although his serve is weak, he is one of the top ten players in the world.

(Dentsu, Tokyo Fast Electric, 6th) Sato Jiro, the main player of the Japanese Davis Cup team, stopped disembarking for recuperation and departed for Singapore on the afternoon of the 5th. However, not long after the departure, on the evening of the 5th, he committed suicide by jumping into the sea from the Hakone Maru. The cause was extreme neurasthenia.

(Dentsu, Tokyo Electric, 6th) According to a telegram from the Tennis Association, Davis Cup player Sato Jiro was missing shortly after the Hakone Maru sailed from Singapore to Europe at 3 PM yesterday. After searching, a suicide note was found in his private room, and it was learned that he had committed suicide by jumping into the sea. When Sato was decided to be the Davis Cup player in January of this year, he suffered from neurasthenia. At that time, it was thought that it was not suitable for him to travel far across the ocean, but when he departed, he had fully recovered. The parties concerned deeply hoped that there would be no problem, but because life on the ship was monotonous, or perhaps because of this, the old illness recurred. When the Hakone Maru arrived in Singapore, the shipowner telegraphed the Tokyo Tennis Association to report, [Player Sato wants to go ashore, how should we handle it?]. The reply was [Go to Marseille]. Sato also had no intention of landing. There was a continuing telegram report, thinking that he felt the responsibility of being the main player, which aggravated his illness. Sato was from Gunma Prefecture and is currently a third-year student in the Department of Political Economy at Waseda University. Since he first attended the Davis Cup tennis war in the sixth year of Showa, he has often attended the international tennis world. In the past two years, he has fought to the semi-finals in Europe. The Tennis Association held an emergency board meeting at 1 PM today, deciding to send a staff member to Singapore and deciding that Sato's funeral would be held by the Tennis Association.

(Dentsu, Tokyo Electric, 6th) Regarding the aftermath of Sato's incident, the Tennis Association decided to send Fukuda Masanosuke to Singapore on the Fushimi Maru, which sets sail from Yokohama on the 15th. It also decided to urge Miki Ryuki to rise again and replace Sato as the main player.
