Regulations for the Exhibition of Labor Science Achievements in Vocational Schools and Primary and Secondary Schools 194

Notice to All Provinces and Cities to Hold Previews on September 1st

On the 5th, the Ministry of Education issued a notice to the education departments and bureaus of all provinces and cities to hold a National Exhibition of Labor Science Achievements in Vocational Schools and Primary and Secondary Schools in Beijing on the Double Tenth Festival this year, which has been reported in yesterday's newspaper. The regulations are recorded below:

Regulations for the National Exhibition of Labor Science Achievements in Vocational Schools and Primary and Secondary Schools in the 23rd Year of the Republic of China 195

Chapter 1 General Provisions

Article 1 In order to collect labor science achievements from vocational schools and primary and secondary schools across the country for comparison and improvement, the Ministry of Education will hold the National Exhibition of Labor Science Achievements in Vocational Schools and Primary and Secondary Schools in the 23rd year of the Republic of China (hereinafter referred to as "this exhibition"). Article 2 All public and registered private senior and junior vocational schools and primary and secondary schools in the country must participate (primary schools may choose to participate). Article 3 The location of this exhibition will be in Nanjing. Article 4 The exhibition period is set from October 10th to 20th in the 23rd year of the Republic of China. Provinces, cities, and districts should hold preliminary exhibitions separately before September 1st. Article 5 When the Ministry of Education deems it necessary for the exhibited achievements, it may seek the consent of the exhibitors to keep them for display in the ministry.

Chapter 2 Preparatory Committee

Article 6 The preparation and holding of this exhibition will be handled by the Preparatory Committee for the National Exhibition of Labor Science Achievements in Vocational Schools and Primary and Secondary Schools in the 23rd year of the Republic of China (hereinafter referred to as "the preparatory committee"). Article 7 The preparatory committee will have 11 to 19 members, who will be appointed or hired by the Minister of Education. Three to five executive preparatory members will be appointed from among the preparatory members to be responsible for daily affairs and to convene meetings. Article 8 The preparatory committee will be divided into the following groups: (1) General Affairs and Reception Group: responsible for documents, general affairs accounting, reception, and guidance for visits, as well as matters not belonging to other groups. It will have one director and several staff members. (2) Collection and Display Group: responsible for the collection, registration, storage, arrangement, and display of exhibits. It will have one director and several staff members. (3) Evaluation Group: responsible for reviewing, evaluating, and rewarding achievements. It will have one chief evaluator and several evaluators. (4) Editorial Group: responsible for editing and advertising matters. It will have one director and several staff members. Article 9 The organizational regulations and detailed rules for the preparatory committee will be formulated separately.

Chapter 3 Scope of Exhibits

Article 10 The scope of exhibits is divided into two parts: main and subsidiary. The regulations are as follows: A. Main Exhibits: (1) Practical achievements and working drawings of vocational school students. (2) Labor achievements and working drawings of primary and secondary school students (such as metalworking, woodworking, dyeing, bamboo working, sewing, embroidery weaving, scientific instruments, biological agronomy specimens, and labor sports teaching aids, etc.). For the above two items, the step-by-step achievements of the manufacturing sequence of the finished product must also be attached, choosing the best. B. Subsidiary Achievements: (1) Achievements of educational administrative agencies (such as the number of public and private vocational schools, the amount of funding, the number of grades, the number of students, the number of teachers and staff, the subjects of vocational and labor science, the qualifications and treatment of teachers, the employment status of graduates, and various investigation statistics related to vocational education, as well as investigation reports on local raw materials and social economy, etc.). (2) School administrative achievements (such as the equipment of practical and experimental places, the quantity of products sold in previous years, statistics and handling methods, the employment status of graduates, and various valuable investigation statistics, etc.). (3) Teaching achievements (such as the curriculum syllabus and practical progress schedule for vocational and labor science subjects, and the research achievements of teachers, etc.).

Chapter 4 Exhibit Procedures

Article 11 The procedures for educational administrative agencies in various provinces, cities, and districts to send achievements are as follows: first, the achievements of each province, city, and district should be pre-exhibited, and then representative achievements should be selected, together with a list of exhibits, and sent to the preparatory committee before September 15th. Article 12 The transportation of achievements will be the responsibility of the educational administrative agencies in various provinces, cities, and districts. The preparatory committee will not be responsible for any accidental losses. Such losses will be borne by the provinces, cities, and districts themselves. Article 13 The format of the list of exhibits is as follows: Category, Product Name, Exhibitor, Number, Quantity, Remarks. Article 14 Each exhibit must be attached with a label in the following format: Product Name, Number, Price, Source of Raw Materials, Exhibiting Agency, Student Name, Production Date, Remarks. The label should be made of white paper. Article 15 The following matters should be noted for exhibits: (1) The drawings and charts to be collected must use high-quality domestic paper or Daolin paper. (2) Artistic works such as Chinese paintings must be selected with large-scale works and properly mounted. (3) Unmounted photos must be at least eight inches in size. (4) Models, specimens, instruments, and other achievements must be properly installed to avoid damage. (5) The outside of the box for framed, porcelain, and liquid exhibits should be marked. (6) If provinces, cities, and districts wish to keep the exhibits for display in this ministry, they should indicate this in the remarks column of the exhibit list. Article 16 Exhibits that are not desired to be kept for display in the ministry will be returned by the original sending agency within one month after the closing of the exhibition.

Chapter 5 Rewards and Punishments

Article 17 Those with excellent achievements will be rewarded by the preparatory committee submitting a request to the Ministry of Education in accordance with the following regulations: (1) Grade A: given a Grade A certificate. (2) Grade B: given a Grade B certificate. (3) Grade C: given a Grade C certificate. Article 18 A province, city, or district or a school with particularly excellent achievements will be commended by the preparatory committee submitting a request to the Ministry of Education. Article 19 Those with excellent achievements will be announced in the special publication of the National Exhibition of Labor Science Achievements in Vocational Schools and Primary and Secondary Schools in the 23rd year of the Republic of China and the Gazette of the Ministry of Education, in addition to the aforementioned methods. Article 20 Those with particularly poor achievements or schools that must participate but have not submitted their achievements without special reasons will be instructed to pay attention by the preparatory committee submitting a request to the Ministry of Education. Article 21 Any matters not covered in these regulations may be amended by the Ministry of Education at any time. Article 22 These regulations will be implemented from the date of promulgation.

The Gengzi Indemnity and Education and Cultural Undertakings (5) 196

The Dutch Gengzi Indemnity 197

1. The Motivation for Returning the Indemnity

In October of the 14th year of the Republic of China, the Dutch government, in order to enhance the friendship between China and the Netherlands, sent a Dutch envoy to present a memorandum to the Beijing government, expressing its willingness to return the remaining amount of the Dutch portion of the Gengzi Indemnity, to be used exclusively for undertakings beneficial to China. They also felt that the Yellow River flood was a serious disaster and intended to use the Dutch Gengzi Indemnity to manage the Yellow River and extend the use of Dutch hydraulic engineers to jointly plan to eliminate the immeasurable harm suffered by the people in Chinese history. The Beijing government immediately expressed its gratitude, but this case was never decided due to frequent political changes.

2. The Mature Period for Returning the Indemnity

It was not until April of the 22nd year of the Republic of China that our government exchanged documents with the Dutch Minister to China, deciding to return the full amount of the Gengzi Indemnity owed to the Netherlands from January 1, 1926 (the 15th year of the Republic of China) to our country, designated for use in Chinese water conservancy projects and to subsidize cultural institutions.

3. The Sino-Dutch Exchange of Documents and Coordination

Regarding the use of the Dutch Gengzi Indemnity, the exchange of documents stipulates very clearly, the most obvious of which are: (1) 65 percent of the returned funds should be used for Chinese water conservancy projects, and the remaining 35 percent should be used for cultural undertakings.

4. The Total Amount of the Returned Indemnity

It is estimated that the Dutch gold is 3,066,055 florins and 289.

5. The Amount Allocated for Educational and Cultural Undertakings

Regarding the 35 percent used for cultural purposes, 400,000 shields should be allocated from the funds that have been accumulated since January 1, 1926 (that is, the 15th year of the Republic of China) and are currently in the custody of the Dutch government as a cultural fund. This fund should be handed over to the board of directors organized by the Chinese diplomatic representative stationed in The Hague and the president of the Faculty of Arts of the Royal Academy of Sciences of Amsterdam and the president of the University of Leiden for safekeeping and handling. In order to enhance Sino-Dutch cultural relations, 53 percent of the annual interest earned by the cultural fund should be handed over to the Chinese Academy of Sciences, and the Chinese Academy of Sciences will use 53.33 percent of its annual interest as a subsidy for the academy's undertakings, and 43 percent as expenses for sending Chinese scholars and students to study in the Netherlands, but the ratio can also be changed if necessary. The remaining 47 percent of the annual interest earned by the cultural fund will be donated to the Chinese Studies Institute of the University of Leiden in the Netherlands every year.

6. The Organization of the Dutch Gengzi Indemnity Board of Directors

The Dutch Gengzi Indemnity Board of Directors is named the Sino-Dutch Gengzi Indemnity Water Conservancy Undertakings Board of Directors. The organization of this association is extremely simple and is only composed of two Chinese directors and one Dutch director appointed by the Chinese National Government, and one of them is designated as the chairman of the board, under the jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan.

7. Current Board Member Candidates

The Chinese side is Shi Ying and Sun Fushi, and the Dutch side is He Longmen. Shi Ying is also the chairman of the board.

8. Recent Status of the Dutch Gengzi Indemnity Distribution

Because the Dutch Gengzi Indemnity has not been returned for long, it has not yet been distributed. (End)

Revision of Regulations Governing Consular Management of Overseas Chinese Education 202

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Education, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission jointly announced the revised Regulations Governing Consular Management of Overseas Chinese Education, consisting of ten articles, on April 5th. The original text is as follows: (Article 1) Resident consuls or vice-consuls (hereinafter referred to as "consuls"), unless under special circumstances, shall manage the administrative matters of overseas Chinese education in their respective resident locations and areas of jurisdiction in accordance with the provisions of these Regulations. (Article 2) The scope of consular management of overseas Chinese education includes the following: (1) Receiving guidance and inspection from the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and handling matters related to overseas Chinese education. (2) Reporting the status of overseas Chinese education to the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission at least once a year. (3) Accepting applications for registration from overseas Chinese schools and overseas Chinese education groups, and forwarding documents to the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for review. (4) Encouraging overseas Chinese to establish educational undertakings. (5) Handling matters related to overseas Chinese children returning to China for schooling. (6) Handling matters related to the commendation of overseas Chinese who are enthusiastic about education. (7) Assisting personnel dispatched by the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission to conduct investigations or manage overseas Chinese education in the respective resident locations and areas of jurisdiction, and facilitating all matters. (Article 3) The handling of overseas Chinese education by consuls includes the following matters: (1) Promulgating central government education laws and regulations, and supervising their implementation. (2) Introducing the party's ideology and educational methods, and directing their implementation. (3) Investigating the number of children in school and the number of children out of school. (4) Investigating the sources and amounts of funding, as well as their management, allocation, budget, and final accounts. (5) Inspecting the administrative, teaching, and training conditions of schools and other groups. (6) Evaluating educational achievements. (7) Guiding educational improvement. (8) Establishing training sessions and research groups to enhance the knowledge and skills of primary and secondary school teachers regarding education. (9) Commending outstanding teachers and staff. (Article 4) Before assuming office, consuls shall consult with the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission regarding all matters related to overseas Chinese education in their area. (Article 5) Consuls, with the approval of the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, may divide their resident locations and areas of jurisdiction into several school districts, designating one excellent school that has been registered with the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission in each district to lead and improve overseas Chinese education in that district. (Article 6) Consuls, with the approval of the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, may appoint qualified personnel from excellent schools or groups that have been registered with the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission in their resident locations and areas of jurisdiction as honorary supervisors to inspect and guide local overseas Chinese education. (Article 7) Each consul may specially hire supervisors and other personnel to manage the administration of overseas Chinese education, with the approval of the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. (Article 8) All matters submitted by overseas Chinese education groups may be reviewed and forwarded by the consuls to the Ministry of Education and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission. (Article 9) Matters not covered in these Regulations shall be jointly revised by the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval. (Article 10) These Regulations shall be approved and promulgated by the Executive Yuan upon joint submission by the Ministry of Education, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission, and shall be implemented accordingly.

Local News

Municipal Party Headquarters Sends Letter to Literary and Art Circles: National Revival as the Central Ideology 204

The Municipal Party Headquarters believes that with the current national crisis becoming increasingly urgent, promoting national revival is an urgent priority. As this city is the cultural center of the country, there are many literary and art writers who promote nationalism, but there are also concerns about ideological biases and conceptual errors. To correct this, the headquarters sent a letter to all literary and art societies, writers, and publishing circles yesterday, defining "national revival" as the central ideology of literature and art. The original letter is recorded below: [Respectfully, in recent years, foreign tribes have invaded and national difficulties have become increasingly urgent. Saving the country and preserving existence is the common responsibility of the people today. Looking around China, the people are lazy and the national spirit is declining to the extreme. In addition, literary and art writers, in their works, either pursue the relationship between men and women or hate the class divisions, or vent their anger and dissatisfaction, or indulge in lustful desires. The cause and effect circulate, serving as each other's complement, so that the national spirit gradually becomes passive, world-weary, romantic, hedonistic, decadent, and dispersed. The power of self-confidence is lost, and the unity of the group is not strong. How can we hope to exert national power to resist foreign aggression and secure internal stability? The rise and fall of the country and the elimination of abuses depend on the joint efforts of the literary and art circles. In view of this, this headquarters has determined that "national revival" is the central ideology of all literary and art this year. Your publication has the responsibility of guiding young people and saving the country. Please express your grand theories according to this purpose to improve the social customs. The country and the nation rely on it. Sincerely,]

Fourth Annual Meeting of the Chinese Sociological Society Opens Yesterday Morning 206

More than 50 people attended, including Sun Benwen.

Pan Guangdan and others presented papers.

The meeting will continue today to discuss society affairs.

The Chinese Sociological Society, established four years ago, held its fourth annual meeting yesterday morning, starting at 9:00 AM, at the ninth floor of the YMCA in Baxianqiao. Papers were presented, and the meeting will continue today to discuss society affairs. The situation is as follows:

Attendees: The attendees included Guanghua University’s Pan Guangdan, Liu Changyi, Qin Ding, Chen Guangpu, Xu Kuangchou, Zhou Xuede, Yuan Keshang, Central University’s Sun Benwen, He Liankui, Yan Xinzhe, Daxia University’s Wu Zelin, Wu Zuhuang, Chen Shaoji, Wu Zeyan, Fudan University’s Ying Cheng, Xu Zhaoxiao, Zhang Chengzhi, Henan University’s Zhu Yisong, and others, totaling more than 50 people. Jiang Jianbai, Section Chief of the Fourth Section of the Education Bureau, attended to provide guidance.

Chairman's Report: Chairman Sun Benwen reported that, when it was the Republic of China year 17, realizing the importance of social science, people initiated the organization of the Southeast Sociological Society. By the Republic of China year 18, professors from various universities in the north believed it was necessary to expand the organization, so it was reorganized into the Chinese Sociological Society. In June of the 19th year of the Republic of China, the first annual meeting was held, and the scale was slightly established. Then, in accordance with legal procedures, it was registered with the Nanjing Municipal Education Bureau and reported to the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Party Headquarters for record. It became a formal legal entity. In recent years, the more important aspects of the work were: (1) the publication of the Journal of Sociology, which has been going on for several years; (2) the holding of annual meetings in the past, the first in Shanghai, the second in Nanjing, and the third in Peiping. This meeting is still held in Shanghai. The purpose of holding the annual meeting is to focus on the presentation and dissemination of papers, so that the members can take this opportunity to publicly report on their research.

Research on Inkstones (18) 217

— Bored Guest

General Situation of She Inkstones

(5) Various Beautiful Patterns: Among the beautiful patterns of She stone from various pits, the dragon tail, golden stars, and spiral patterns are the most precious. Dragon tail stone without patterns uses golden stars as patterns, and these three kinds of beautiful patterns have numerous names and strange patterns. Literary scholars and scholars often like to play with them, but the Stone Forest Summer Retreat Record once said that She inkstones have lacked good materials for a long time, and dragon tails are no longer what they used to be, and spiral patterns and eyebrow patterns are no longer seen. This shows the preciousness of these three kinds of stones. Therefore, they are described in detail below.

1. Dragon Tail Stone: Produced in water, it is firm, dense, warm, and moist. The sound is clear and melodious like jade. The color is dark black, with varying shades. It is particularly good if it is smooth and has many edges. The stone pattern with golden stars is the most precious. (1) The most precious is when the stars are tightly clustered like a dragon's tail, (2) The stars that are dotted like morning stars, (3) The ones that are as dense as sprinkled gold, (4) The ones with fine circles like falling flowers, (5) The ones that are all gold skin are the worst. Golden stars are always dominated by glittering gold, and pale yellow is not worthy of being precious.

2. Spiral Pattern Stone: The predecessors said that the spiral pattern stone starts ink better than the dragon tail. The color is blue-green. The slightly finer coarse spiral pattern is easier to grind ink. The slightly harder fine spiral pattern produces the most ink. It is also said that the spiral pattern is like rice grains, moist, dense, firm, heavy, and flawless. It is the wonder of inkstones. The spiral pattern names recorded in the Inkstone Note are a total of twelve kinds, which are listed below.

Fine Spiral Pattern: The most moist and warm with a blue color, and it is considered upper-grade without stars.

Dark Fine Spiral Pattern: The stone is blue-black and not exposed. It can only be seen when placed in water.

Ancient Rhino Spiral Pattern: Slightly finer than the horn wave pattern.

Gua Zi Spiral Pattern: There are spots like melon seeds.

Stone Heart Spiral Pattern: There are subtle fine lines hidden in the center of the stone.

Golden Star Spiral Pattern: The dots are like stars and as thin as eyebrows.

Golden Halo Spiral Pattern: The halo has several layers like a painting.

Golden Flower Spiral Pattern: There are gold-plated flowers on the fine lines.

Strand Spiral Pattern: Slightly like the lines in the palm.

Brush Silk Spiral Pattern: The lines are slightly rough, like brushed with a broom.

Pine Pattern Spiral Pattern: Like the texture of pine wood, slightly brownish-yellow.

Pebble Spiral Pattern: Like an oval shape with blue skin and yellow skin.

The Inkstone Note also states that the coarse spiral pattern, black nail, horn wave, and abacus are not recorded, so it can be seen that the above-mentioned twelve types are only the best ones. However, when we study She inkstones, we cannot limit ourselves to the best ones. Therefore, the discarded sub-products are also recorded below.

Coarse Spiral Pattern: The eyes are slightly rough and the stone texture is not very fine.

Abacus Spiral Pattern: Also known as abacus strips, like bamboo in an abacus.

Horn Wave Spiral Pattern: Like triangular water wave patterns.

Date Heart Spiral Pattern: Like a date pit shape, there are two types, thick and thin.

Raindrop Spiral Pattern: Like falling rain, also known as black nail pattern.

Fish Roe Spiral Pattern: Like small fish traveling in groups.

The above are the sub-products of the spiral pattern. The spiral pattern is divided into interior mountain and exterior mountain. The predecessors only said that the golden stars of the interior mountain spiral pattern are sparse and slow, and the exterior mountain spiral pattern is similar to the fine spiral pattern and slightly rough. However, how to distinguish between the interior and exterior mountains is very rarely seen by us, and I am ashamed that I cannot explain it in detail.

Shen Bao Radio Weekly

A Chart for Inspecting the Reactance of Inductors and Capacitors 218

— An Ignoramus

Sometimes, to know the reactance of inductors and capacitors in order to determine the alternating current values in radio frequency and audio frequency circuits, these two formulas are commonly used: (1) To find magnetic inductive reactance XL = 2πfL; (2) To find capacitive reactance Xc = 1/(2πfC). Calculating using these two formulas is quite cumbersome and prone to errors due to the decimal places involved. Now, there is a chart for inspecting the reactance of inductors and capacitors. If the capacitance of the inductor and capacitor is known, its reactance can be found immediately, which is very convenient. The diagram is as follows:

[Space]

Capacitance ( )

Usage

This chart is N-shaped, divided into three sections: A, B, and C. Section A is for wavelength. Section B is divided into two subsections: (1) and (2). Subsection (1) is the magnetic inductive reactance to be inspected, and subsection (2) is the capacitive reactance to be inspected. Section C also has two subsections: (1) and (2). Subsection (1) is for inductance, and subsection (2) is for capacitance. Usage examples:

(1) An inductor has a capacitance of one hundred megahenries. What is its reactance at a wavelength of 100 meters?

Solution: First, find the one-megahenry point on subsection (1) of section C. Then, find the 100-meter point on section A. Use a ruler to intersect these two points on section B. The magnetic inductive reactance at the intersection point is approximately L00 ohms, which is the desired value.

(2) A capacitor has a capacitance of 0.0002 farads. What is its reactance at a wavelength of 100 meters?

Solution: Similar to the first example, find the 0.0002-farad and 100-meter points. The capacitive reactance at the intersection point is found to be approximately 265 ohms.

If the reactance of a certain inductor and capacitor is known at a certain wavelength, its inductance and capacitance can be inspected on the chart.

— Jiancun

In a radio, the power amplifier is a part that consumes a lot of power. If batteries are used, the cost is quite high, which is somewhat unsatisfactory. With the invention of the eliminator, the function of the power amplifier in AC radios has gradually become widespread.

The vacuum tube is the main component required for a power amplifier. The vacuum tube used must have a characteristic that can withstand a sufficiently wide range of grid voltage amplitudes. Commonly used tubes are UX171A, UX210, UX250, UX245, UX202, etc., among which the UX245 is the most common.

The first diagram shows a power amplifier, which is the final stage circuit in a radio. The relationship between its AC input voltage and AC output voltage can be determined based on the following four important characteristics:

(1) The amplification factor of the vacuum tube; (2) The plate resistance of the vacuum tube; (3) The total load impedance of the plate circuit (Load impedance); (4) The DC voltage of the grid and plate.

Radio-Controlled Battleships 220

— Ming Xiang

The ink on the international peace treaty is not yet dry, and all countries are painstakingly preparing for the next World War. Continental countries such as France, Italy, the United States, and Russia are concentrating their efforts to develop their land and space authority, while Britain, in order to maintain the glory of its naval supremacy, is constantly seeking new methods to command its navy.

British naval experts want to use radio to control their battleships from a considerable distance, so that their actions are completely under command. Not only that, but in wartime, all the work on the ship, such as firing guns, launching cannons, laying mines, and releasing smoke bombs, is controlled by radio, without the need for a single soldier. This dream began in 1925 and has been continuously tested, and has now been largely successful.

Although the principle of radio remote control is extremely simple, the equipment is extremely complex. A signal is emitted from the control station using a specific wavelength (similar to the transmitting device of a radio telegraph). The controlled battleship has a highly sensitive receiving device that is pre-tuned to the wavelength of the control signal. When this signal is received, the output current of the radio causes a weak jump, which can activate a corresponding relay. The closing of each relay can affect the steering compass, causing the battleship to sail in a certain corresponding direction, and the actions of each relay can be completely controlled by different signals.

Controlling the sailing of a battleship is relatively easy. The most difficult task is to control the use of weapons on the battleship, such as loading ammunition and aiming (this work may be done by radio transmission in the near future). After a long period of experimentation, a relatively simple machine has now been invented to make aiming extremely effective. First, two circular transparent sheets are installed on an airplane, each of which is divided into several degrees and numbered. At the same time, a table track with the same degrees and numbers is also set up on the controlled battleship. The reconnaissance pilot on the airplane looks at the target to be bombarded below through this circular sheet. If the enemy ship is found at a certain degree on the circular sheet, say four, he immediately sends a signal [four] to the control ship. The control ship immediately uses radio to calibrate the table track on the battleship so that it is also four, and then fires the cannon. At this time, the reconnaissance pilot on the airplane must pay attention to the point where the cannonball lands. If it is very close to the enemy ship, the splash can be observed through the circular sheet at the adjacent number, say five. Immediately send another signal [five] to the control ship. Then, the control ship uses radio to control the table track on the battleship again, so that the range of the cannonball is appropriate. If the reconnaissance plane directly controls the battleship, it can be even faster.

In future wars, a large fleet of warships can be controlled by radio from a very light and fast small boat, so that all actions are under the command of the commander.

On Low-Frequency Amplification 221

— Qi

Low-frequency amplification (Audio Frequency Amplification) occupies an important part in larger radios that use loudspeakers for sound reproduction. It has a significant impact on the overall efficiency of the radio, especially in terms of the volume and sound quality of the radio's output. Its quality entirely depends on the low-frequency amplification stage, so it is essential when designing a radio. However, novice radio researchers often fail to achieve excellent results due to a lack of understanding of the characteristics of various low-frequency amplification configurations and improper installation. In view of this, the author ventures to provide a simple explanation of the commonly used low-frequency amplification configurations, hoping that novice comrades can learn from them.

(Diagram 1)

(1) Transformer Coupling Amplification (Diagram 1) This type of amplification configuration is the most common, as it can obtain high sound amplification with only a small amount of power. However, when combined with a powerful output tube, the increased B voltage can easily cause distortion. If designed comprehensively—such as correcting the grid voltage and adding shunt capacitors—distortion can also be reduced.

(Diagram 2)

(2) Resistance Coupling Amplification (Diagram 2) This amplifier consists of a non-inductive resistor connected with a fixed capacitor. Because this type of resistor can maintain its constant value at any frequency, even when used in high-level amplification and final-stage power amplification, its output can still be distortion-free. Its sound quality is excellent, clear, and far superior to that of transformer amplification.

(Diagram 3)

(3) Push-Pull Amplifier (Diagram 3) If you want strong sound, excellent sound quality, and no distortion, this is the only option. Generally, large-power radios and pickups use this type. However, due to its excessive power consumption, ordinary small-scale radios do not use it much. Moreover, since the invention of the pentode power tube, researchers generally believe that a single-stage audio frequency power amplification is enough to enjoy.

The above three low-frequency amplification configurations are the most common. In addition, there are (Loftin-White) direct coupling amplification and transformer-resistance coupling amplification, etc. Due to space limitations, they will be described in detail for readers on another day.

Voltage Doubling Method for Rectifiers 222

— An Ignoramus

When rectifier tubes are used in ordinary rectifier circuits, using half-wave or full-wave rectification can only increase or decrease the ripple current. It cannot increase the output DC voltage to twice the AC voltage supplied to the plate before rectification. Now, if a special circuit is used, it can produce a DC voltage that is exactly twice the original AC voltage. This connection method is called the voltage doubling method for rectifiers.

Diagram 1

Diagram 1 shows a half-wave rectifier tube connected in a voltage doubling method.

If a triode is used to replace it, the grid must be connected in parallel with the plate. If a full-wave rectifier tube such as 80 or 82 is used, the two plates must be connected in parallel. If the input AC voltage to this rectifier is 110V, the output DC voltage can reach around 240V.

Diagram 2

Diagram 2 shows the voltage doubling connection method for a 25Z5 voltage doubling rectifier tube.

The principle of voltage doubling is easier to understand with reference to Diagram 2. Because the two plates of this tube have two capacitors C1 and C2 connected across them alternately, the change in positive and negative polarity is used, as if two half-waves are connected together. When plate P1 is rectifying, capacitor C1 connected across plate P2 is discharging. Therefore, the combined output DC voltage is the sum of the plate voltage of the rectifying plate and the discharge voltage of the capacitor, which is exactly twice the original input AC voltage.

The installation of the filter is the same as usual. C1, C2, and C3 are 4-microfarad filter capacitors that must withstand a high voltage of 400V. The inductor is 30 henries. A voltage divider resistor can be connected to the output DC voltage to adjust to an appropriate voltage.

(Note) For radios that use this type of voltage doubling rectifier and whose AC power supply for the plate voltage is directly taken from the live wire (i.e., without using a step-up transformer), if a ground wire is used, a 1-microfarad high-voltage capacitor must be connected in series with the cathode to prevent the rectifier tube from short-circuiting and being damaged.

Inductors and Capacitors 223

— Shi Huaxin

Inductors and capacitors are important components of AC-powered radios. Their function is to filter out the ripple in the rectified DC current, transforming it into a very pure DC current. Therefore, the two are called the filter stage in the rectifier.

An inductor is the same as an ordinary coil, but the inductance used in a rectifier must be very large—approximately 30 henries. Therefore, the center is made of iron core. In high-quality inductors,

(1) there should be an air gap because its inductance is much larger than that of the same inductor without an air gap.

(2) The DC resistance should be small, otherwise the voltage drop will be too large when current passes through it, and the output voltage will be greatly reduced. Although the output voltage of the rectification part can be increased to compensate, it is often not possible to increase it excessively due to the rectifier tube, which affects the results.

However, for the sake of simplicity, the excitation coil is used instead of the inductor in radios using electrodynamic loudspeakers, which is also very suitable. However, the resistance of the excitation coil is very large, so the voltage drop is also large, and the output voltage of the rectification part must be increased during design.

When in use, inductors are mostly connected to the positive side, but the effect is still very good when connected to the negative side.

The capacitors used in this part must have high voltage resistance and large capacitance, and the price must be low. There are usually the following three types, each with advantages and disadvantages. If they are properly matched, the effect is almost the same.

1. Mica-insulated capacitors: They can withstand very high voltages and are very suitable for filtering work. However, the value is extremely high, and it cannot be purchased by amateur enthusiasts.

2. Electrolytic capacitors: They take up very little space and can save on the volume of the radio. However, the voltage resistance is not high, about 400 volts, so when used in voltages higher than 400 volts, several must be connected in series. For example, connecting two of the same capacitance in series, the voltage resistance is 800 volts, and the capacitance is only one-half of each. If configured properly, the value is not expensive, and the effect is great. As for the service life, according to the manufacturer, it can be used for eight or nine years, but it is usually damaged due to excessive voltage. This type of capacitor has positive and negative polarity when connecting, so pay attention when using it.

3. Paper capacitors: This type of capacitor is the cheapest, and the voltage resistance is also low, about 200 volts. It is very suitable for use in small radios, and it can also be connected in series like electrolytic capacitors. It is said that the service life is only one or two years, but according to my experience, if the voltage does not exceed the specified value, it can also be used for several years. This type of capacitor is not used much in the power supply part of imported radios. Electrolytic capacitors are commonly used. The biggest use is as a bypass capacitor, such as being connected in parallel with a resistor to replace C battery, etc.

Points to Note When Making Your Own Power Transformer 224

— Bing Yi

Amateur enthusiasts who study radio should focus on interest and economy, so when playing with AC machines, they prefer to make their own power transformers. However, when winding such small transformers, the following points should be paid attention to so that its efficiency can be high and it is also very durable.

(1) Accurate design: Regarding the design aspect, this magazine and other magazines have detailed guidance, which will not be repeated. However, when designing, you should pay attention to whether the frequency applicable to the iron core in the winding table is the frequency of the local power supply. For example, if the table states that it is suitable for 60 cycles, and the local frequency is 25 cycles, then the iron core area must be increased to 2.1 to 2.2 times to be sufficient, or the number of turns per volt must be increased. However, power generators rarely use frequencies below 50 cycles.

(2) Accurate wire selection: Most of the wires wound in the power supply framework are enameled wires, because they are cheap and small in size. There are usually two types sold on the market: SWG (British Standard) and B&S (American Standard). The two wires of the same number have different current carrying capacities. The British Standard NO. 20 enameled wire has exactly the same current carrying capacity as the American Standard No. 19 enameled wire. The British 30-gauge wire is equivalent to the American 28-gauge wire, so when buying wire, you should match the standard used on the table so that there will be no loss in any aspect in terms of economy, position, and durability. (To be continued)

[A Child Blocks the Way] 226

— Mi Zizhang

In the past five or six years, foreign movies first showed us the bravery of foreign heroes, then the inferiority of barbarians, and then the curved beauty of foreign ladies. But our horizons are expanding, and eventually a few legs are not enough, so there is a large expanse; and then it is not enough, so there is nakedness. This is [Nude Movement Grand Photography], although it is a proper [Expression of Human Beauty and Healthy Beauty], it is also [A Child Blocks the Way], they are not worthy to see these [Beauty].

Why? There is such text in the promotion —

[A very smart child said: Why don't they turn their bodies around?]

[A very upright father said: No wonder theaters block children!]

This is of course just a wonderful text imagined by a writer, because the film is marked with [A Child Blocks the Way] from the beginning, and they have no way to see it. But if they really let them see it, would they ask such questions? I think, maybe they will. However, the meaning of this question is probably completely different from what Zhang Sheng sang [Alas, why don't you turn your face around?], it is actually the unnatural attitude of the people in the movie that makes him feel strange. Chinese children may be relatively precocious, or maybe they are more sensitive to sex, but they are not as unclean as their adult [father]. If this is the case, the Chinese society twenty years later would be truly terrible, but in fact it will probably never be the case, so the answer is better changed:

[Because they want to make me unsatisfied, how hateful!]

But there are probably not many [fathers] who are willing to say this. He always has to [use his own heart to measure the hearts of others], and after measuring, he forcibly stuffs this heart into the cavity of others, pretending that it is not his own, and saying that the hearts of others are not as clean as his. The nude women all [do not turn their bodies around], in fact, it is specifically to deal with this type of people. Are they idiots, don't they even know that the eyes of the [father] are more unruly than those of his children?

However, Chinese society is still a society of [fathers], so the plays are performed by the [mothers] dedicating themselves and the [sons] being slandered. Even at the critical moment, it is still something like [Mulan Joins the Army], [Wang Yi Defends the Country], to push out [women and villains] to perfunctorily deal with the situation. [How can our people take care of their future?]

Random Thoughts 227

— Xia Chang

(18)

Liu Dasheng's theory of [Being an Official and Acting in a Play] says: [The most serious thing in the world is called being an official, and the most illusory thing is called acting in a play. But I am very foolish. Every time I see singing, crying, laughing, scolding, fighting, and joking in the theater, I recognize it as real. The truth is not in the disguised ancient people, but in the actors who play the ancient people, each with parents, wives, and children, each needing to support their families, each using crying, laughing, fighting, and scolding to support their parents and support their wives and children. These actors are true ancient people. And every time I put on a crown and belt, dress up and act, I am indeed a true official, and no one in the world suspects me of being an actor. It is not known that the officials who bow and sit, have joyous faces and smiling mouths, and those who put on a stern face and are awed by their majesty, are actually these ancient people who support their families, cry and laugh. They take a theater, props, script, and acting style, and use their entire internal organs for the play, and they themselves are not aware that they are true actors. Alas!] Exposing the peep show, tearing off the mask, I wonder what kind of feeling the current officials will have when they read it, will their skin crawl all over? Dasheng is too bad, isn't he? A smile!

(19)

Literary people often have strange ideas, and the poor often open up new avenues, completely irrational. For example, the aforementioned filling of hunger with nature is one example; Tang Yi's theory of the jar is also an excellent article. He said: [My sick body is drifting and there is nowhere to return, so I will stay in a lonely temple. There is a bed in the temple but no quilt, and there is a quilt in the inn but no mosquito net. Now I ask the monk to borrow a fish tank, and I sit and lie in it day and night. Friends pity me and stop me, and often warn me not to speak. If the ancients used a jar as a bed, then I have a bed today but no jar, and you should pity me for not having a jar. Having a bed makes me know the pain of not having a mosquito net, but if I don't have a bed, what can I ask for a mosquito net? Please comment on this situation, what do you think of the text?] This kind of speculation, although not whimsical, is also to his credit for thinking of it.

[Vernacular] [Classical Chinese] New Discourse (Continued) 229

— Cao Juren

Originally, the rise of vernacular Chinese was greatly influenced by Western literature. Therefore, the sentences in vernacular Chinese became complex in structure, often containing many adjectives, adjective phrases, adverbs, and adverb phrases (the so-called Europeanized style). For example, in Guo Moruo's translation of Goethe's *The Sorrows of Young Werther*, there is a sentence:

[When the beautiful valley around me steamed, the bright sun shone on the densely shaded forest, only two or three rays of light stole into the holy place within the forest, I would lie on the deep grass beside the stream, and the countless fine grasses on the ground would cling closer to the ground and be noticed by me: my heart would feel even more closely the buzzing of the small world among the grasses, the uncountable and inexhaustible kinds of insects and gnats, and I would feel the existence of the Almighty; He created us according to His form; I would feel the breath of the All-Benevolent, He supports us floating in this eternal joy.]

The entire sentence contains 158 characters. The first adverbial phrase (from "when" "then") has 42 characters, and it also contains three short clauses, each of which contains many "words" and "phrases." This complex structure was not found in classical Chinese before. In European literature, not all adopt such a complex structure. For example, in a Nordic narrative cited by Lafcadio Hearn, there are only ten adjectives in 750 words. However, complex structures are common in the literary styles of England and Southern European countries. (Wu Guangjian's translation of Dumas's *The Count of Monte Cristo* into classical Chinese deleted many sub-clauses or straightened out compound sentences.) Vernacular Chinese, influenced by Europeanization, has made sentences very complex, which we should recognize as a kind of progress.

In fact, the complexity of modern writing and the simplicity of ancient writing are inevitable considering the tools used and the objects described. Zhang Shizhai said: [Ancient people wrote books on lacquered bamboo slips, or on silk, or with knives to scrape off mistakes. It was cumbersome and unbearable, so the writing was concise and strict, with no redundant sentences in the chapters and no redundant words in the sentences. This was because writing was difficult, so they were forced to write only to express their meaning sufficiently. They not only disdained being verbose, but also had no time to be verbose. Now that paper and pen are used for writing, it is ten times easier than using bamboo, silk, and knives. The verbosity and rambling nature of writing can then be done as one pleases. Although there are inherent shifts in the style and quality of writing with the times, it is common for people to be indulgent in what is easy and convenient, and to be cautious and strict when it is difficult and cumbersome.] (Yimao Notes). He has pointed out the connection between tools and writing style. Now that mechanical industry is booming and tools are readily available, their convenience is a hundredfold greater than in the Qianlong and Jiaqing periods. It is inevitable that writing styles will become unrestrained. In classical Chinese, Wang Anshi's ten-thousand-word memorial was already considered a grand spectacle. Today, when people write, such as Liang Qichao's preface to Jiang Baili's *History of the Renaissance*, it is written to sixty or seventy thousand words. This is something that ancient people could not have dreamed of. In the past, writers lived in rural agricultural societies, leading simple and leisurely lives. The objects they wrote about, such as nature and small towns, changed very little. At the beginning of writing, they considered carefully; after writing, they revised carefully. They could do such fine polishing work to make the articles appear very concise. Now, the metropolises created by industrial society have too complex lives and too rapid changes. The old saying describing the crowding of cities was [cars like flowing water, horses like dragons]. Using this to describe the streets of Shanghai today is not entirely accurate. The old saying describing the evening scenery was [ten thousand homes lit up]. How can the [ten thousand homes lit up] describe the [red] colored neon of Shanghai's night scene today? Since the words and phrases used to describe things in the past are exhausted, the large increase in adjectives and adverbs is a necessary product of the times. Today's writers in big cities, as soon as the ink touches the paper, the manuscript is sent for typesetting, with no room for maneuvering. Those engaged in the news business sometimes do not even have the leisure to consider. The rambling nature of words and phrases is a factual necessity. Therefore, the lengthiness of words and phrases can be said to be a shortcoming of vernacular Chinese, but it can also be said to be a strength of vernacular Chinese. It is still difficult to say whether it is right or wrong. (To be continued)

[Don't Know] 230

— Zang Kejia

｜Room Without Windows, Essay Three｜

Yesterday, I mentioned a very popular female celebrity to a village school principal. He shook his head and said:

[Don't know]!

I didn't say anything, but my expression probably showed something, and he said very bluntly: [What, too ignorant]?

[Too ignorant]. This sentence touched me, and I felt very uncomfortable, so I found some more things from this.

If you talk to a country person about the fluttering figures in a dance hall, or about people moving and talking on the screen, he (or she) will be as surprised as if hearing a heavenly book. If you tell him that a meal in the city costs tens of dollars, he will definitely stick out his tongue.

The people in the countryside, in today's situation where economic bankruptcy is like quicksand that cannot be held back in a rapid current, are struggling for a living in poverty, barely holding on with only a single pair of pants to fight against the cold north wind. Nothing else can reach their hearts. People living in the city can only take the bankruptcy of the countryside as a term. If you ask him what it looks like when it's bankrupt, if he's honest, he'll answer: [Don't know].

I remember in the high-rise buildings of the school, when I was bored on winter nights, I would call a worker to pour a pot of tea. Then, with the red stove fire, everyone would gather around, each lying in an Andover chair, smoking a cigarette, and various opinions would slowly emerge from the smoke. You approve of this ideology, I sympathize with that [style], and we seem to become enemies. At first, there's a little noisy debate, but later we simply argue with red faces and pound the table, each seeming to have won the oral battle, and that ideology or [style] can be realized immediately. As a result, everyone suffers from insomnia.

This is a kind of verbal ideology. An after-dinner pastime [style]. If you ask what the current situation in the countryside is, I'm afraid no one [knows]. Not only are university students like this. There are many works written about the bankruptcy of the countryside right now. If you are a real country person, those three words will shut the writer's mouth! Because what he writes is imagined or observed from a transcendent position.

Generally, people sing loudly about rural relief, but while singing, they can't help but do things that further accelerate the speed of bankruptcy. In their eyes, rural bankruptcy is on the statistical numbers. If you ask them about the real situation, it's also:

[Don't know].

Half a Day's Work (5) 233

— Li Huiying

The slowly moving队伍 finally finished Weixin Street and walked onto Henan Street. This is the busiest street in the whole city. Usually, there are countless pedestrians, but at this time, it is even more crowded, cutting off traffic. I don't understand what these people are watching! No, they are probably watching female students. Female students have always been the object of appreciation and evaluation by these leisurely docile people. Of course, they are unwilling to give up this rare moment of right.

Clearly, I heard people on the side of the road criticize people in our team:

[That little guy is really good-looking, his eyes are so lively].

[The one with the thick calves is also good, your vision is not good].

[No, the one wearing patent leather shoes is still good, the willow waist is very flirtatious].

At the same time, I also heard someone cursing with pain:

[Enjoying themselves, such decent slaves of a conquered nation]!

[What's there to see? The more you look, the more angry you get. Pleasing the Japanese]!

[Ah! Time passes so quickly, it's been almost two years].

Hearing these kinds of words turned all the anger in my stomach into sadness, but from this, I clearly saw that the people's hearts have not completely died. One day, the large group of oppressed slaves will turn over.

All the rickshaws and horse carriages on the street were hiding on the side of the street, unable to move. The police were driving away the improperly dressed crowd. Smoothly, in a short while, the team arrived at the stadium.

There were more people in the stadium than on the street. The following twenty characters were posted high on the gate:

[Commemoration of the 19.18 Two-Year Anniversary and Celebration of the 9.15 One-Year Recognition Anniversary].

Police and military police were constantly pushing back the crowded audience. Our team calmly walked into the gate of the stadium.

The military band played music frantically, not knowing whether it was celebrating our arrival or praising our obedience. Before long, the students from First Normal School, First Middle School, First Workers' School, County Middle School, Midwifery School, Municipal Elementary School, and County Elementary School also arrived. If we compare today's situation with the grand meeting held here two years ago, the only difference is that a group of new guests have been added to a corner of the stadium, namely the students from the Japanese Tongwen Commercial School and the Japanese Elementary School. In the past, no students from these schools participated in the grand meeting. There is also an opposite fact revealed in the stadium: after the teams of each school were arranged in a certain position, it could be seen that in the teams of Japanese students, small national flags were constantly waving, and people were full of energy, showing excessive happiness, jumping, shouting, and laughing. And we, the students of the conquered nation, regardless of middle school students or elementary school students, were almost all standing there dejectedly, thinking, not jumping, not shouting, and not crying, like a group of idols.

Such a phenomenon is rare. At least, these students have not forgotten their own shame, but what is the use of just passively being sad?

It's getting hot. The autumn sun is especially difficult to bear when it shines on people, and with the people watching the excitement all around, men and women, it's so crowded that even taking a breath seems very difficult. The noisy situation is not like a meeting place about to begin, but like an open-air theater performing a wild opera. After a while, a child cried, after a while someone cursed, and after a while someone made a strange noise. It can be said that their interest in coming here is similar to going to the Beishan Temple Fair on April 28th. The only difference is that they may still have a small hope hidden in their hearts, that is, to admire the demeanor of the noble officials and important people.

Farming is Difficult, Eating is Also Difficult 238

A Farmer's Stone of Rice Endures a Thousand Hardships and Sorrows

How Much Can Be Earned with Sweat and Blood

Because of the reduction of the斛司's (measurement office) small fees, a situation of 斛停 (suspension of measurement) has occurred, which has been going on for two days. This cannot but lead to thinking about the various expenses of a farmer's stone of rice coming to Shanghai to sell. The farmers have exhausted their hands and feet in planting rice, but unexpectedly, they suffer a lot of losses in selling it. This is such pain!

Because they cannot directly find consumers, they have to invest in buying and selling. It is understandable that brokers collect commissions for selling on their behalf. As for everything else, although it is said that it is all paid by the brokers, this money does not belong to the brokers. The wool comes from the sheep. Ultimately, the loss is borne by the seller, and the seller is the ultimate bearer - the farmer.

Not to mention other places, just take the example of transporting rice from the interior to Shanghai. The external expenses for a stone of rice are as follows:

(1) Water freight 1.5 corners This is an average approximate number. In reality, it ranges from as little as 1 corner and 1 or 2 to as much as 1 corner and 7 or 8.

(2) 斛力 (measuring force) 24 wen This is the labor fee that the broker pays to the 斛司. In reality, it also comes from the seller.

(3) Small account 3 points This is a kind of tip that the seller pays to the 斛司, which is now open.

(4) Sticking to the car 3.5 points This is a kind of tip for carrying from the rice boat to the car on the pier.

張袋(bag spreading) 10 wen This is for the broker to use for the coolies.

(5) 回船(return boat) 568 wen This is the return money that the broker gives to the boatman after the rice 斛 is unloaded clearly. Based on a boat, it is calculated at 200 stones per boat, which is equivalent to 3 wen per stone.

(6) 經售(selling through) 5 points That is, the seller who sells goods to the broker from the seller's hand also takes commissions from it.

(7) 行佣(brokerage commission) 2 corners This is the commission money charged by the broker, but 6 points of it is returned to the rice shop as loading and unloading fees, etc., and after deducting miscellaneous fees of about 1 point, the broker actually receives about 1.3 corners.

(8) 耗米(rice consumption) 2 sheng This means that the seller delivers one stone of rice to the boatman to sell in Shanghai. In addition to paying the water freight, the boatman must also deduct 1 or 2 sheng of rice per stone as consumption. That is, the seller actually receives only 98% of the silver for one stone of rice. If the rice price is calculated according to the current rice price, it is already 1.6 corners. The higher the rice price, the greater the income.

In addition, there are public office donations, 2 wen for Changbang and 7 wen for Nanbang. That is, the above-mentioned various expenses have been calculated to be 6.4 corners, which is the loss of the farmers and also the increased burden of consumers.

Compared with 30 years ago (calculated at 1,000 wen per yuan), the cost per stone at that time was as follows:

Brokerage commission 7 points 斛力(measuring force) 4 wen 斛司小帳(斛司 small account) 1 point 駁力(駁力) 0.012 經售(selling through) 1 point

Although there are still water freight, etc., there is a much bigger difference compared to now.

Therefore, if a farmer adds taxes, land taxes, and local donations to a stone of rice, how much can he earn at the current rice price? To relieve the rural areas and help the farmers, there must be practical efforts.

Cargo exchange miscellaneous payments collected and delivered more than 2.3 million, and 500,000 were shipped out. The money house collected and delivered more than 39 million foreign public orders. Yarn and Cotton 242

Marked Yarn Sees Profit-Taking and Short Covering 243

The yarn market fell in the morning and rose in the afternoon. Actual demand was slightly active, with the most diligent procurement still from the Southern ports. Other domestic ports were less enthusiastic, but selling prices were still difficult to raise due to excessive inventory and competitive sales among factories. As prices rose, selling increased. Judging from the market situation, the period of continuous decline was too long, triggering profit-taking and short covering, resulting in a rebound of two to three yuan.

This Month's Cotton Futures May See a Short Squeeze 244

The cotton market, which had been falling for many days, rose by four rupees due to the rise in Indian cotton during the holiday, but American cotton was average. Therefore, a certain bank absorbed a large amount of cotton and firmly refused to release it. It is rumored that there will not be much delivery, and there may be a short squeeze later. The market rose as a result, but the cotton market is unlikely to rise significantly due to the slump in the yarn market.

Grains 246

Northern Guild's Strong Procurement Drives Period Flour to Rise Sharply and Cover Shorts 247

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning, was driven by the Northern Guild's heavy procurement in recent days, successively loading several ships with spot flour. Yesterday, they inquired about spot and futures in the market, which triggered short covering and long buying. The market atmosphere was very active, and sentiment was particularly good. All months rose in unison, especially the current month, which was more active and popular due to spot flour. However, it was briefly suppressed by factory selling. The closing price rebounded due to hoarding and short covering. The final closing price was up two cents for the current month, one and a quarter cents for the next month, one and a half cents for June, one cent for July, and three-quarters of a cent for August. The initial opening price for September was $2.055, followed by a slight drop of a quarter of a cent. There were no transactions in the afternoon.

The Lonely and Desolate Period Wheat 248

There was little trading in marked wheat yesterday, and all parties lacked enthusiasm. There were few transactions throughout the day, and prices did not fluctuate much. Imported wheat was quoted down by one to two jiao. Previous orders continued to arrive in Shanghai, but sentiment remained unchanged. There was little trading in June, July, and August period wheat in the upper and lower markets. The closing price remained similar to the end of last month. Spot wheat has not been traded for more than a week. Yesterday, Fuxin Huafeng handled more than 30,000 packages of wheat to various routes, with prices three to five cents lower than at the end of last month, including Sucai wheat at 3.5 yuan, Linhuai at 3.57 yuan, Xuzhou at 3.55 yuan, and Bengbu at 3.45 yuan. Secondary grades were reduced accordingly.

Late Indica Rice Shows a Slight Soft Trend 249

Hubei Side Still Not Opening the Dou

(Shanghai South Side) Yesterday, the sources from various guilds were still scarce, only about 30 firms (over 5,000 shi). Sales in various markets were sluggish, and the situation was unusually quiet. Customer guilds, such as the Southern Guild, have already stopped, and the Northern Guild has suddenly become sluggish again. Therefore, although sellers want to make the market appear popular due to the scarcity of goods, they ultimately have no way to do so due to sluggish sales. Moreover, those who want to move prices will not do so without thinking of cutting prices first. As a result, although the market has been held up by sellers again, only six to seven hundred packages of Qingjiao, Silian, and other late indica rice were purchased. Although prices did not fluctuate much, the trend has softened. The market appetite in this street's shops is average. The prices of early japonica rice from the Chang Guild, Sutong, and Nangang remain at old levels, with little difference. The movement of Du Yangjian rice is flat, but fortunately the supply is scarce, and it is still stable. The balance of supply and demand is similar to before.

(Shanghai North Side) Because the customer guilds want to reduce the small accounts of the dou managers, the problem has not yet been resolved. Yesterday, the measuring of grain was still suspended. The dou managers' measuring fees have always been 24 wen per shi given by the firms, and the customer side also pays a small account of 3 cents per shi, but secretly it has been more than that when rice is expensive. Recently, the customer guilds wanted to reduce it, initially negotiating to reduce it to 2 cents per shi, but the dou managers refused. Then there was talk of increasing it to 2.5 cents. The dou managers believe that this small account of 3 cents has already been filed with the government and is no longer comparable to old malpractices. Therefore, they insist on not giving in. Seeing the firm attitude of the dou managers, the customers also expressed that they would not back down after a meeting. With both sides holding out, the rice market has been suspended.

Increasingly More Passenger Xian Rice Arriving 250

Passenger Rice Still Strong... Stocks Are Also Thick

Yesterday, Min Guild still had a greedy appetite for guest rice. This street in Wenzhou was also inquiring. The market and sentiment are all trending upward in unison. However, two new batches of Xianggan passenger indica rice have arrived, and there are still goods on the way in the near future. Although the cargo owners want to raise prices, they are also restricted by the situation. Therefore, except for the high-grade rice, which is still insisted on a limited price, the middle and lower grades are all sold at market prices. The situation is similar to the previous market. A total of 3,793 packages of various types of rice were opened in the whole market, with Fuzhou accounting for the majority. It is estimated that there are 700 packages of Jiangxi machine-milled early and late rice, 1,264 packages of Hunan machine-milled rice, 400 packages of Shashi brown rice, 629 packages of Mingguang and Wuxi machine-milled rice, 236 packages of Wuhu machine-milled rice from Wenzhou, and 64 packages of Hunan broken rice and 500 packages of small patterned rice from this street. The prices are all similar to the previous market, but the high machine late and other types were not successfully delivered due to unsuccessful price negotiations. There are still more than 120,000 dan of rice in stock in the whole market.

Divide and Conquer 270

— Qiong Sheng

A storm is brewing, and recently the Japanese warlords, in order to cope with the crisis of the coming years, are trying hard to break through the difficulties. They are advancing both with [Manchuria and Mongolia] and implementing diplomatic [total mobilization]. Under this goal, they say they are actively working with the countries concerned, understanding the domestic situation and the Japanese government's policies. They have tried to recall ambassadors from the United States, China, and France to their country to receive instructions in person. It is said that this refreshed diplomatic policy has the significance of preventing the allied countries of the Washington Conference from uniting against Japan and conducting separate negotiations to recognize the puppet regime. Therefore, it is named: [Divide and Conquer Strategy]. The principle of its implementation is based on the premise that all countries will recognize the puppet organization before 1936.

Divide and conquer, this is obviously a new policy in Japan, because we are now happy to have won the sympathy of the world, declaring that Japanese diplomacy has fallen into isolation. Especially by clinging to a resolution not to recognize the puppet organization and some kind of agreement, we have long been at ease, [covering our ears and ignoring the affairs of the world, shutting our doors and only reading ancient books]. It goes without saying that we have a heart that loves peace and a purpose of appeasement. But is this divide and conquer strategy of the wooden clogs friends feasible?

The answer to this question is both affirmative and negative. We affirm it because, in the present situation of being busy preparing for war on the eve of a major war, the anti-Japanese camp of the great powers can indeed suffer [divide and conquer] under Hirota's diplomacy. Can the great powers sit idly by and watch Japan's expansion and monopoly of the Far East? Of course not, but each has its own concerns. The British Empire, as the eldest of the production machinery, cannot compete with the rising star of the United States in negotiations. Therefore, not only in Latin America, does it have great contradictions with the United States, but its colonies around the world are also gradually developing [centrifugal force]. This aging psychology makes it want war, but also fear war. Although it is envious of Japan's seizure of Manchuria, it may be subjected to Japan's [divide and conquer] under the [reluctant maintenance of the status quo]. The United States also needs a temporary [transformation] of US-Japan relations because its naval construction plan has not been completed, and it has huge conflicts with Britain on a global scale, in order to consolidate its power in Latin America and prepare for the overall solution of the Far East issue. As for France, its economic position and military strength in the Far East are maintained by the [fair treatment] and [friendly relations] of Britain, the United States, and Japan in the Pacific, and will not make Japan's policies feel constrained. As for countries like Italy and Germany, they are even more out of reach. Therefore, in general, it is possible to realize the [divide and conquer] policy.

What is the negative significance then? It is that the temporary [defeat] of the countries by Japan is only to further accelerate their preparations for war. When a war to redistribute the market breaks out, I am afraid that this policy will not be able to achieve its ultimate goal. Because it is very obvious that if a Far East war occurs to compete for the market, it will naturally be to divide up this vast and resource-rich ancient country. If the conflict between the great powers is caused by the monopoly of the Manchurian and Mongolian economy, then the current [divide and conquer] magic weapon will probably not work.

However, the wooden clogs friends have their cleverness here. They will take on the role of the vanguard in attacking the red monster to obtain the recognition of various countries for [Manchuria and Mongolia], and also use this to make a fuss in order to achieve the goal of encroaching on North China. This is probably the reason why the situation in North China is becoming more critical when Hirota is singing loudly about rational diplomacy and [divide and conquer]. A certain evening newspaper reported that Zhang Ji, a member of the Central Committee, said: The crisis in North China is fraught with dangers, and Beiping is in danger of being lost at any moment, similar to the situation in the Northeast before [September 18th]. He believes that the day of becoming slaves is already in sight, which is the truth.

The Paris Qingyi Daily said, [Japan has no scruples about China, because since the North China truce in June 1933, Japan has firmly believed that a Sino-Japanese understanding will not be difficult to achieve]. I wonder if this understanding is that we are being [divided and conquered] under [total diplomatic mobilization], or if it is another matter, which remains to be seen.

Sunset over Qiantang 271

— Qingmu

In the dark night, before the east had fully revealed its fish-belly white glow, the roosters crowing in the next yard had already stretched their necks and crowed endlessly, startling me from my slumber. At that time, I was still lazily falling back into sleep, but they raised their voices even higher and warned me like a mad cry: [Traveler, wake up quickly! Have you forgotten that you only have today to stay? You haven't seen the beautiful scenery of the sunset over Qiantang from the Jianggan embankment. If you miss today's opportunity, the next time will be unpredictable! ]

I took the coal-eating contraption to Jianggan, and sat on the Liuhe Pagoda and looked into the distance until sunset. Ah! I'm afraid that any place with good scenery can't compare to the serenity and transcendence of this place. The continuous small mountains like blue snails on the water surface, the few returning sails at the junction of the sky and water, and the shimmering waves like the eyes of a virgin, are all enough to dispel my worldly thoughts. In this infinitely beautiful sunset, in the embrace of such great nature, I forgot all the darkness of the future.

The beautiful scenery of the setting sun over the Qiantang River, none of its beauty is unlike a peerless beauty. Are those few faint distant mountains that are lightly drawn, not like the beautiful eyebrows of a beauty? Are those rose-like clouds in the western sky, not like the blushing cheeks of a beauty in her beauty and shyness? Is the sound of the wind blowing on the waves, the wonderful aftersound, not also like the beauty's clear and crisp throat? The few returning sails facing the wind are like the light and graceful posture of a beauty walking. The scenery at dusk is becoming more and more beautiful. A round of red sun has already half entered the heart of the river, the surrounding mountain peaks have become vaguely indistinguishable, and the golden light flowing on the waves is like ten thousand swimming golden snakes; it is also like countless flashing shooting stars in the sky. I am afraid that even if Muse were to be reborn, she could not describe its beauty even to one ten thousandth.

The returning boats are dotted, rising and falling in the ripples like seagulls. The spring-hearted girls on the boat are singing their clear voices, singing and swaying the songs of free love. They are truly immortals in the mortal world. No matter morning or evening, in the midst of that green water and gentle waves, no matter how affectionate and happy they are, no one will know or interfere. It's a pity why I wasn't born here and become a fisherman, but was born in this vast world!
