The True Meaning of [Nude Movement] 273

— Tian

Turning, turning, the wheels of this era. Humans are [fond of novelty and tired of the old]. From nudity to covering the body with leaves, from knowing how to cover the body, they have evolved step by step, all the way to wrapping the entire body and only exposing the hands and face. It seems that [wearing clothes] is boring, long clothes become short clothes, simplicity evolves into complexity. Women even [turn over three times a season]. The clothes of a year don't know how many times they have to be turned over. The one garment that is enough is no longer applicable. [Things reach the end of the road], and enough turning has been done. So they degenerate again, and gradually some people advocate [returning to the primitive] and being naked!

[Naked] Those two words are so touching. The whole group takes off completely [not a single thread]. You look at me, I look at you, the whole body is exposed. Women have always considered [the mysterious breasts] and [the incredible reproductive organs]. At this moment, they are [regardless of everything] completely naked! It's good, if you really return to such a situation, [class consciousness] will be less divided. Walking on the road, no one will see her as a young lady, or her as a maid. Who can tell [XX is a rich man], or [XX is a poor man who [cannot eat his fill]]! To put it playfully, the arresting officer's baton should be more careful when it is used, lest it accidentally touch the [inviolable] noble.

Although that's how it's said, after there really is such a fact, the clever [supermen] will come up with other tricks. After all, status must be divided, and [mixing pearls with fish eyes] is not the end of the matter. So they turn from nudity to other tricks, and the concluding sentence, [returning to nature], is still just a bourgeois fashion!

If you recognize the true meaning of [returning to nature], seductive advertisements have long been despised by people. If it is really as the advertisement says, isn't it the same as spending money to see mysterious pornography? Taking [nude movement] as a novelty, taking it as an exhibition of the body. Inevitably, in this metropolis that is filled with strong eroticism, [public exposure of the body] is just a timely [stimulant]. Speculators take advantage of this opportunity to publicize it greatly, surprisingly exceeding [all content], and the audience is willing to pay a considerable price in exchange for a short period of [satisfaction of the eyes], especially the [spring-hearted] youth, after seeing the seductive advertising text, involuntarily [their hearts swaying and their spirits shaking], and are confused by the eye-catching words of [reproductive organs publicly exposed]!

This is what is called a reflection of a part of the true meaning of the current [nude movement]. This impression is ultimately a terrible impression, entangling the wrong target, blurring the eyes, confusing the will, and numbing everything else.

It is true that the wheels of the era are turning. If the words [nude propaganda] were mentioned in a Chinese film three years ago, it would have been banned long ago. But today, not only is it not banned, but it is allowed to be shown publicly. Undoubtedly, this is the wheel of the era turning forward. Some people also believe that this is turning backwards, because its name is [returning to nature]. This is another question, which will be put aside here for the time being.

The future is unpredictable, maybe the [nude movement] will really succeed one day. This depends on how the situation arises. I expect that even if it succeeds, it will be difficult to maintain it for long. If it loses its true meaning, it will only be harmful! Because everyone exposes [reproductive organs], [reproductive organs] will become as ordinary as the current [hands]! Seeing them with your eyes also makes it easier to take action. When a certain [sensitivity] takes effect, its bad consequences are more likely to occur!

The goal of [returning to nature] is currently recognized as the vanguard of [healthy body]. It also took on this title and called on others, but looking at it from the current perspective, it is simply to implement this in order to see [reproductive organs]. If that is the intention, I might as well plan a kind of clothing as follows, I think it will be much faster than the nude movement Female - A long cheongsam with a large round hole dug out at the crotch of the pants, and the buttocks should be made completely naked, as should the breasts, or made into long, square, or triangular shapes, or other exquisite patterns.

Male - For those in suits, cut a small hole in the crotch of the pants that can drag out the reproductive organs, and there is no need to expose the face. Those wearing long robes can imitate the female style.

On Reading 274

— Qian Preface

The purpose of reading is, of course, different for everyone, but everyone thinks of using it as a tool to obtain a comfortable life.

The ancients' [ten years of cold window] was to [ascend to a high position] and today's [studying abroad] is to obtain a [doctoral degree]; although there are plenty of people who read ten thousand books and still remain a student their whole lives, and those who get a doctorate degree may not all become high officials – which is to say, they fail to achieve a "comfortable life." That is just an example of the ancient and modern [poverty and success are destined, wealth and rank are in heaven], a helpless thing, truly fate.

[Books] must be read, and people today generally agree that reading is the only [way out] for an individual. So, shouldn't the methods of reading be discussed?

In the past, the Four Books and Five Classics were required reading, the foundation of everything, and advancement depended on them. But now, times have changed, who would bother with these stale things? Although the [revivalist] gentlemen are still willing to rummage through antiques to find treasures, few people pay attention in the end. Unfortunately, apart from the fixed path from enlightenment to elementary school and middle school, beyond that, there are many forks in the road and it is hard to know what is right. Some people use [interests] and [aspirations] to determine their future, but none are as clever and brilliant as using means to obtain a [comfortable life]. If you really want to take [serving the country and benefiting the people] as your own responsibility, then you are a very, very big [fool].

Because China has very few [fools], those who study medicine overseas come back to delve into literature, and those who study military affairs raise the banner of politics high upon their return.

Does reading ultimately need guidance? Those who guide are of course the wise and perceptive, and those who are guided are of course those who are aware later, or even those who are unaware. The [guidance] mentioned here, of course, means that the wise and perceptive tell the later-aware or unaware how to live a [comfortable life] (note: there is a narrow and broad definition), which is to say, how to read and what to read. Lin Yutang strongly disapproves of reading needing guidance and is also a strong opponent of school education. His reason is that [learning and thought slowly gestate and grow, just let it take its course, and do not force it]. And especially do not [force others to read what I like to read]. Liu Zhiji being able to read the Zuo Zhuan but not the Ancient Text Book of Documents is one example. So he advocates finding and reading the articles of the ancients that are close to one's own temperament.

In fact, reading with guidance is not a bad thing, as long as the guidance is appropriate, so-called [guide it according to the situation]. For example, when Zhiji could not read the Ancient Text Book of Documents no matter what, wouldn't it have been a good thing if someone had guided him to read the Zuo Zhuan? Fortunately, he heard his classmates read the Zuo Zhuan and liked it, so he easily memorized it. If he had never heard anyone read the Zuo Zhuan in his life, wouldn't he have wasted an excellent talent? Therefore, especially those who are wandering on a fork in the road and have not yet developed the ability to discern, desperately need proper guidance.

Mr. Lin Yutang said in the February issue of Shen Bao Monthly that reading must have courage, vision, and perseverance. I believe that reading must also have a goal, because with the former, there is only objective criticism, and with the latter, there is a subjective understanding.

Public Servants and Entertainment Venues 275

— Ying Dai

The Dawn of the New Life Movement

According to reports, since Chairman Chiang initiated and implemented the New Life Movement, no soldiers have been taking rickshaws in Nanchang these days, and civil servants have disappeared from tea houses, restaurants, brothels, and entertainment venues. If this is true, then we cannot but acknowledge the success of the New Life Movement!

Originally, when we went to Nanjing, Zhabei, especially the interior, tea houses, restaurants, brothels, and entertainment venues, which place did not have the footprints of civil servants? Logically, civil servants should be role models for citizens, but now civil servants are the first to engage in these degenerate activities, how can citizens not imitate them?

Having become a civil servant, as long as you have epaulettes on your shoulders and a badge on your chest, you can ride in a car without paying, watch a play without paying, and drink tea and alcohol without paying. The so-called forced borrowing and buying is truly doing all kinds of evil and doing all kinds of bad things!

In our hometown's entertainment venues, whenever there is a drama or movie, the best seats are taken up by civil servants, soldiers, and police early on. The brilliance of badges and epaulettes shines in all directions. With a talisman, watching a play for free, no one dares to speak. In the theater, they also gesticulate wildly and disregard others, often causing trouble.

Ah! Civil servants should be role models for the people, but now... They should maintain local order, but now, not only do they not maintain order, but they also disrupt it. The so-called holding a position without performing duties, being a thief to the people, has long been obvious to everyone!

Therefore, if we want the Chinese people to know propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, to change their usual degenerate and decadent state, and to abide by the New Life... It is truly not recognized to start with civil servants!

Now, because Chairman Chiang is in Nanchang, Nanchang is starting to rectify things. As a result, no soldier is taking a rickshaw again, and civil servants have completely disappeared from tea houses, restaurants, brothels, and entertainment venues. But apart from Nanchang, the military and political authorities in all other places should... Observe regulations, otherwise, what use is it to only have Nanchang?

Spring Night 276

— Zi Yan

Pushing open the window of the small building, the breeze gently brings fragrance in. Looking out from the window, the sky is a hazy expanse, stars twinkle, and the songs coming from the courtyard stir in the quiet air. One will leisurely lean back in the writing chair, smoking a Turkish cigarette, close one's eyes, and think of all the things that one would never think of at ordinary times.

This is a spring night.

The spring breeze twirls around the loose hair of ladies and dances on the purple flower ties of gentlemen. Special spring tour buses take large groups of urban men and women to breathe the air of spring in another world. It brings a light and lively mood, and everyone is immersed in the embrace of spring.

Several young people came out from seeing "Cloud Garments and Dazzling Tunes" in Nanjing, and their legs lightly slid onto Avenue Joffre, stepping into the Russian cafe. Large steaks, stimulating alcohol, flirting with the waitresses with abandon, sorrow falls behind joy, enjoying this spring night that is worth a thousand gold pieces as much as possible.

Staggering out of the cafe, the neon lights shine on my flushed face, singing, laughing, like sailors, rickshaws gather around shouting [immediately write].

[When there are flowers, pluck them, don't wait until there are no flowers and break the branches in vain.] A foreign girl smiles and pays attention to us, she does not understand the meaning of the words and the reason for our laughter. My right hand approached my lips and sent a kiss, she said娇嗔a Nansehce, as moving as music. Spring, this is the season of happiness, we can only laugh, how much joy is there in life, do not fail the good spring light; have fun, this spring night.

Several people, shoulder to shoulder, stepping with heavy steps, marching like the military, heading west on Avenue Joffre. The Avenue Joffre at night is full of temptation, the dark green lights in the shops on both sides illuminate women's underwear, spring fashion models, young people's hearts beating wildly, and sin is probably where it begins to capture its prisoners.

Walking and walking again, chasing out every pedestrian, gradually the sound of trams is no longer heard. The night is deep, inevitably turning back [let's go back]. Women's underwear and spring fashion models are no longer seen in the window displays, and the music in the cafe is also lazy and not as energetic as before. The Russian woman touched our shoulders and said [Lovemetonigbt].

Returning, collapsing into the writing chair. Gazing at the sky in a daze, leisurely thinking of many lovely stories, she is like the spring night, fleeting and no longer traceable.

[...Come back, sweet dream...] The songs from the neighboring courtyard are endlessly sent by the spring breeze. Immersed in a sweet dream... Have fun, do not let down...

Scholars and Officials 277

— Song

In the imperial examination era, the government selected scholars through literature, and scholars became the superior class in society. The so-called [all professions are inferior, only studying is noble] is clear evidence of the general public's respect for scholars. Scholars received special treatment from the state. As long as they were familiar with the books of the sages and learned the skills of writing eight-legged essays, seeking official positions and ennoblement was not a difficult task, at least much easier than for ordinary commoners. Scholars were in this win-win situation, advancing to become officials, retreating to become refined people, as commoners, still remaining respected scholars. It can truly be said that scholars were people above people. Moreover, it is said that scholars have always been noble, despised the secular world, and had no interest in officialdom, which are all beautiful stories left for posterity to praise. The famous Tao Yuanming refusing to bend his waist for five pecks of rice, preferring to resign and return to the fields, is undoubtedly a typical figure representing the noble scholars of ancient times.

Due to the shift in the tide of the times, the scholars and officials of ancient times had a close relationship. As long as they were loyal and devoted, the emperor's grace was vast, and they would not have to worry about not having an official position to take. But coming down to today, scholars have lost their former status in the eyes of the general public, and their social status is even more filled with feelings of the past and present. Moreover, in this era of natural selection, scholars cannot survive as a leisurely class as their predecessors did. In the past, scholars would not take official positions, but now they seek official positions but cannot obtain them. As for characters like Tao Yuanming who show off their nobility, of course, there are none.

Some say that although there is now an Examination Yuan established to identify talent, select the wise and capable, and allow heroes to have a place to use their skills, so as not to arouse feelings of not being recognized, this cannot but be called a step for scholars to advance. However, among thousands of people, being fortunate enough to be hired is rare. Even if elected, there are few real official positions, but rather a title that has a name but no substance. A blank check, the realization of which is indefinite, and waiting on an empty stomach, there is no real benefit to speak of. Being an official or not being an official, there is no difference.

Scholars are full of learning and have a brilliant writing style, and it is not difficult to express upright and serious opinions, but in the end, their power is no more than talking on paper, and it does not help in practice. Because today is an era of military-national democracy, everything rigid, marching in square steps, and intellectual egg sacs are mostly eliminated. The reason why scholars cannot hold an official position is not due to the government's discrimination, but because the scholars' own strength is weak, and they are not worth anything. Writing and reciting poems, and manipulating ink, are the only true colors of scholars. Apart from this, they have no other strengths. Alas, scholars, how can they deal with themselves?

Novel

Siamese Anecdotes (6) 278

— Yi Min

Naked Women

The dress of Siamese women is very simple. In the city, most of them wrap a piece of floral cloth around their lower body, and only loosely wrap a three- or four-inch wide white gauze around their breasts. Some don't even use white gauze, and their breasts are completely exposed. Those young girls occasionally wear a gauze vest, which looks to have a unique charm. As for shoes and socks, they don't need them. Even aristocratic women, when going out, only put on a pair of leather slippers on their bare feet. However, metal ornaments are indispensable for them. Even a female vendor carrying a betel nut stand must wear a gold or silver belt around her waist. Those who have more money always have one or two diamond rings on their fingers in addition to the gold belt. Speaking of places farther away from the city, it is said that most of them still live a completely naked life.

What needs to be added here is the diligence of Siamese women. Whether it is farming, fishing, or carrying scallions and selling vegetables, it can be said that it is the duty of women. Men stay at home to hold children and cook. Therefore, the words [At home, obey your father, when married, obey your husband, when your husband dies, obey your son] do not apply to Siamese women. Not only do they not need to rely on men, but in fact, men rely on them.

Rainy Season and Floods

The weather in Siam is truly strange. Not only is it hot like summer all year round, but it also rains at a fixed time. Starting in mid-September, there is usually a heavy rain every day at noon, and after about two hours, the sky clears after the rain. This lasts for more than a month, which is the so-called rainy season. Starting in November, it will not rain until the next September. During this rainless period, residents in places without rivers are very worried about drinking water. Therefore, during the rainy season, they store water in underground cellars for use during rainless periods. (The above describes the situation inland. In Bangkok, there is tap water, and residents will not feel this kind of pain.) Sometimes, when the water runs out, they have to use ox carts to buy it dozens of miles away, but the price is also very expensive. An ordinary kerosene tank of fresh water costs as much as four or five 角 of silver coins in China.

About a month after the rainy season, it is the flood season. When the water comes, it is also at noon. Clearly a street, in the blink of an eye, it will turn into a river. When returning home in the evening, the ground is very dry again. This lasts for almost three or four weeks. When the tide is high, boats can travel on the streets. Therefore, Siamese houses, even on land, must be built on wooden stakes five or six feet high, like cages, for fear of being washed away by floods. However, Siamese agriculture really benefits a lot from the floods. Because after a flood, many river mud, fish, shrimp, and other things will remain in the fields. In this way, artificial irrigation can be avoided, and the fertilizer that increases the burden on farmers can also be saved.
